1935.04.07

Various Circles in Jiangxi Province Commemorate Deceased Soldiers; Over a Thousand People Including Representatives from the Central Government Participate; The Entire Province Lowers Flags in National Mourning 1

(Nanchang) A grand meeting held by various circles in Jiangxi Province to commemorate deceased soldiers who died suppressing bandits and loyal martyrs was held at the Nanchang Lizi Society on the 6th at 8 AM. The venue was solemnly and respectfully decorated. Eulogies and elegies from central government officials were displayed in the memorial hall, while thousands of elegiac couplets from various places were hung outside the hall, appearing entirely white from a distance. During the meeting, Cheng Tianfang, the central government representative, and fifteen others were elected as the chief sacrificial group, with Yu Baiqing as the chairman of the meeting. Over a thousand representatives from various provinces, cities, troops, organizations, and groups attended. After the meeting began as scheduled, a public memorial ceremony immediately commenced. Cheng Tianfang represented the central government, Xiong Shihui represented Chairman Lin, Gu Zhutong represented Chairman Jiang, and Gong Xuesui represented President Wang, followed by representatives from the province's party, government, and military, who offered public sacrifices successively. The ceremony concluded at 9:30 AM. In the afternoon, public sacrifices were offered by various provinces, cities, organizations, and groups, which lasted until dusk. The provincial capital and various cities and counties lowered flags on the 6th. Plain lanterns and white decorations were hung at the entrances of shops, and entertainment and banquets were suspended. At 11:00 AM, all citizens stood in silence for three minutes to express their condolences. The railway station, bus station, and major streets were decorated with plain colorful arches. Police and boy scouts were fully mobilized to maintain order around the venue and streets, strictly enforcing the rules of the New Life Movement, highlighting a spirit of order and solemnity. According to the chairman's report, Jiangxi Province was plagued by bandits for eight years, with approximately 20,000 soldiers killed in action and over 80,000 loyal martyrs who died in service. Fortunately, Chairman Jiang personally supervised the suppression of bandits from Yunnan and Jiangxi, finally pacifying the bandits in Jiangxi and rescuing the people from hardship. The martyred heroes bravely sacrificed themselves for the nation and the people. Therefore, holding a memorial meeting to mourn the nation is of great significance. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

(Nanchang) The meeting to suppress bandits was held on the morning of the 6th, which, coinciding with the National Tomb Sweeping Day, added to the solemnity. During the meeting, the Film Division of the Central Propaganda Department filmed the event. Airplanes soared overhead, scattering propaganda leaflets. As representatives left the venue, they also distributed historical materials about the suppression of bandits in Jiangxi and special publications from the meeting for commemoration. Gu Zhutong scheduled a luncheon for the sacrificial representatives on the 7th. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

The Three Provinces’ Bandit Suppression Armies Vigorously Annihilate the Red Bandits While Capitalizing on Their Victories 2

(Guangzhou) After the Yunnan, Hunan, and Guangxi reinforcement troops arrived in Guizhou Province, they joined the battlefield to attack the communist bandits in northern Guizhou. This is the largest battle in China in recent years. Seeing that the access to Guiyang was blocked, the communist bandits are now retreating eastward, apparently seeking to join forces with He Long's communist bandits in Hunan. Guiyang is now free from danger. Therefore, foreigners who sought refuge in Anshun will return to the province within a few days. Our troops are now taking advantage of the victory, dividing into three routes to attack the bandits from the rear and encircle and annihilate them. (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

Zhang Xueliang Arrives in Luoyang 3

(Luoyang) Zhang Xueliang flew from Wuhan to Luoyang on a Ford plane on the 6th to attend the graduation ceremony of the third military training class of the Luoyang Military Academy. In the afternoon, he visited the Central Plains Social Education Museum with Zhu Shaozhou. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

(Hankou) Zhang Xueliang flew from Nanhu, Wuchang, to Luoyang by plane on the morning of the 6th to represent Chairman Jiang at the graduation ceremony of the military academy's military training class. Few people knew about it beforehand, only a few senior officials of the headquarters were present to take care of things. It is said that Zhang will not stay in Luoyang for long and will return to Wuhan immediately after the ceremony. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Li and Zhang Return to Chongqing After Their Trip 4

(Chongqing) Li Shizeng and Zhang Jingjiang returned to Chongqing on a civilian steamer on the 6th after enjoying the hot springs in Beibei. The Department of Education invited Li Shizeng to give a lecture at the Social Hall at 3:00 PM on the 7th. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Chen Zhang Discusses the Complete Eradication of Bandit Troubles in Southern Jiangxi 5

(Hong Kong) Chen Zhang returned from southern Jiangxi to the province on the 5th and stated that the remnants of Li Zongbao's gang are currently surrounded in the area between Rucheng and Guidong and cannot escape, annihilation is imminent. The main bandit forces in southern Jiangxi have been completely suppressed, with only a few hundred people remaining between Nankang and Xinfeng, posing no significant threat. (Special dispatch, 6th)

Various Circles in Chahar and Suiyuan Publicly Commemorate Deceased Soldiers 6

(Beiping) A telegram from Zhangjiakou on the 6th reported that various circles in Chahar held a ceremony to pay tribute to deceased soldiers at the newly built Guan Yu Temple on Xitaiping Mountain on the morning of the 6th, which was National Tomb Sweeping Day. Song Zheyuan presided over the ceremony and delivered a somber speech. Men Zhizhong spoke about the brief history of Qingming Festival, and Zhang Wenmu of the Party Committee spoke about the significance of the National Tomb Sweeping Day. Afterwards, a tree planting ceremony was held on the mountain behind the temple. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

(Taiyuan) All leaders of the Jin-Sui Army and officers above the rank of major held a public memorial ceremony for deceased soldiers outside the East Gate today. Over a thousand people attended, and the ceremony was very solemn. It was decided to build a memorial monument there to commemorate them forever. (Special dispatch, 6th)

(Jinan) Today, Han Fuqu held a memorial service for deceased soldiers on Pipa Mountain. Over a thousand representatives from the government and military attended. Han gave a speech and hosted a luncheon. (Special dispatch, 6th)

The Mongolian Political Affairs Committee Plans to Convene a Plenary Session 7

(Beiping) The second plenary session of the Mongolian Autonomous Political Affairs Committee has been scheduled to be held on the 23rd of this month in Bailing Temple. According to related sources, this session will be expanded and enlarged. Sonam Dargye, the deputy leader of the Left Wing League of Qinghai Mongols, and Suhide, the Prince Dorokov of the Right Wing Banner of Qinghai Cholos, have been notified and invited to attend. However, since Prince So is currently in Beijing for a pilgrimage and is expected to stay for a considerable period, he may not be able to attend as scheduled. Therefore, it is still uncertain whether the Mongolian Political Affairs Committee meeting can be held on schedule. (Special dispatch, 6th)

(Taiyuan) Sandayev, the director of the Mongolian Political Affairs Committee, went to Hebian yesterday from Mount Wutai to visit Ge. He will come to Bing tonight. (Special dispatch, 6th)

Mongolia and Suiyuan Both Accept Methods to Resolve Tax Disputes; Prince De Arrives at Pangjiang to Meet Song and Xiao 8

(Beiping) Li Zhizheng, the representative of Suiyuan Province, came to Beiping to discuss the resolution of the Mongolia-Suiyuan tax dispute with Shi Huayan and other parties. After He Binggong drafted five methods for resolving the dispute, they were telegraphed to Mongolia and Suiyuan for compliance. Both parties have expressed their obedience. After Li completes his public duties in Beiping, he will return to Suiyuan and bring the documents of the resolution methods. After reporting back and receiving orders, he will implement them accordingly. Shi Huayan will stay in Beiping for several more days. After Yan Xishan returns to Bing from Hebian within a few days to resume his duties, he will go to Jin to visit him, report on the land reclamation situation in Suiyuan Province, and ask for instructions on the direction of progress. (Special dispatch, 6th)

(Beiping) Prince De Arrives at Pangjiang to Meet Song and Xiao. (6th)

(Beiping) Bao Yueqing received a telegram from Prince De yesterday stating that when the princes of Qinghai pass through Beiping to the temple, he should be ordered to accompany and take care of them along the way. (Special dispatch, 6th)

(Taiyuan) Wang Jingguo returned to Bing from Beiping tonight and is scheduled to go to Hebian tomorrow to visit Yan, report on the resolution of the Mongolia-Suiyuan tax dispute, and lay the foundation for the burial of Yan Shutai. According to reports, he will not stay in Bing for long and will return to Suiyuan immediately. (Special dispatch, 6th)

(Beiping) Because Song Zheyuan is going to Pangjiang and it is necessary to discuss the Chahar border issue with Zhu and Prince De, Prince So plans to return to the league within a few days. If Song can stay in Pangjiang for a short period, he will be able to meet and discuss with him. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Wang Zanxu's Troops Capture Another Important Location; The Bandit Suppression Army in Northern Sichuan Takes On a New Formation 9

(Chongqing) Wang Zanxu, the commander-in-chief of the Sixth Route Army of the Sichuan Bandit Suppression Army, captured Laoya Rock and Ma'anshan yesterday. The bandits retreated towards Bai'aozi. Xu's division was ordered to concentrate in Xiyuan to await orders. Tian, Zhang, and Liu's brigades marched towards Suining. The bandit suppression army in northern Sichuan took on a new formation. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

How Should Guizhou Implement the Three Principles of the People? Work Together to Build a New Guizhou; Eliminating the People's Suffering Requires First Banning Opium; Secondly, Developing Agriculture and Mining; Chairman Jiang's Instructions at the Welcome Meeting of All Circles in Guizhou 10

Guiyang (Late arrival) Chairman Jiang attended the welcome meeting of all circles in Guiyang on the 1st and delivered instructions entitled "How Should Guizhou Implement the Three Principles of the People?" The original words are as follows: Elders, fellow countrymen, and comrades of Guizhou, my visit to Guizhou this time is only for a very short time. I have not had the opportunity to meet and talk with everyone in detail. After the military arrangements are in order, I will invite everyone to meet and talk more often. Today, I am very ashamed to receive such a welcome from the elders and fellow countrymen of all circles. Because for several years, the country has been in a state of internal and external troubles, and we have not been able to fulfill the central government's responsibilities to many places, especially to Guizhou. Therefore, our Guizhou is still the same as it was in the past and cannot make much progress. The central government is truly very sorry. I hope that from now on, the people of Guizhou Province can all strive and work hard under the leadership of the central government, be healthy citizens of the Republic of China, and be true followers of the General to build our new Guizhou and our new nation, and fulfill the revolutionary responsibilities that everyone bears. Regarding how we should relieve the suffering of the people of Guizhou in the future and how we should build a new Guizhou and make it a field for the Three Principles of the People, the central government is very willing to accommodate the opinions of fellow countrymen and comrades from all walks of life as much as possible, and also hopes that fellow countrymen and comrades from all walks of life will contribute more opinions. We know that not only are the people of Guizhou suffering now, but the people in every part of China that I have seen are also suffering. Although there are many reasons for the suffering, the biggest ones are no more than two: one is the impact of bad military and political influences, and the other is that the general public lacks knowledge, self-cultivation, and strength, and does not know how to invigorate and save themselves. Therefore, if we want to relieve the suffering of the people, on the one hand, the central and local governments must do their best to rectify the military and improve politics to relieve the suffering of the people. However, relying solely on a few officials in the government cannot achieve this goal. It is necessary for the general public to be able to awaken, strive, and work together under the guidance of the government to achieve the goal of relieving suffering. Whether they are in the same province or the same place, the comrades of the central government are doing their best to find ways to relieve the suffering of the people and protect the lives and property of the general public so that everyone can live and work in peace and be well-fed and well-clothed. This is the goal of our party and our revolution. One of the purposes of my visit to Guizhou this time is to supervise the suppression of the Red bandits and to protect the people of Guizhou, that is, to protect the production of the people of Guizhou so that everyone can live and work in peace. Step by step, the General's doctrine must be able to achieve this goal. It is necessary for all the fellow countrymen in Guizhou Province, especially the intellectuals and the backbone of society present today, to be able to jointly support the central government and help the implementation of all the central government's policies in order to fulfill the responsibilities of the people themselves. As long as everyone can work together with one heart and one mind, I believe that the suffering of the people of Guizhou can be completely relieved, and a new Guizhou and a new China can be built very quickly. This is the most sincere expectation of the brothers for all the fellow countrymen and comrades. In addition, there are two important meanings that I would like to take this opportunity to contribute to everyone. First, there are many, many sufferings of the people now. It is impossible to completely relieve them all at once in reality. Therefore, it is necessary to distinguish between the priority and urgency, and find the most painful and worrying things for the people and eliminate them first. I think that the most painful and worrying thing for the people in Sichuan or Guizhou now is opium. Not only are those who smoke opium very painful, but those who grow opium are also painful. It not only harms for a while, but also fundamentally endangers the life of the nation. Therefore, whether we want to save ourselves, save others, save the people, or save the country, we must make a firm determination and resolutely ban opium. Not only is smoking prohibited, but also planting and selling are prohibited. This is the most urgent thing at the moment. It is necessary to be able to handle this matter first, and then we can talk about everything else. I believe that none of you present here will suffer from the pain of smoking, but all of you are intellectuals, the prophets and pioneers in society. You should teach the general public who are later aware or unaware, and especially think of all kinds of ways to help them quit opium, which suffers the most and causes the most harm. If our general public can quit opium, their bodies and minds can become stronger, and all new undertakings can be done with effort, and they can progress day by day. At the same time, all the land that used to grow opium will be changed to grow rice, wheat, cotton, silkworms, so that production can develop, and the people of Guizhou can be well-fed and well-clothed. In short, now we want to save the country, we must first save the people, to save the people, we must first relieve the suffering of the people, and to relieve the suffering of the people, we must first quit opium, which is the most painful and harmful to the people. After this point is achieved, everything else will be easy, because after the people quit opium, they can cheer up, improve their morals, and increase their knowledge and abilities, and they can build a good society and government. Other things such as abolishing harsh taxes, developing industries, and improving education can of course be done one by one. This is the first point that the brothers want to contribute today. Second, people generally say that Guizhou is the poorest province, but I don't believe this. I think that the situation in Guizhou is not particularly poor compared to other provinces. The land is very fertile, and all the places where opium can be grown are the best arable land, which can be converted to grow other agricultural products. There are also very rich mineral deposits underground, whether it is coal, iron, gold, silver, tin, oil, or mercury. These national treasures are very abundant. In the future, as long as the people of the province can use the gold, silver, time, and energy that were consumed in smoking opium in the past to mine minerals and develop industries, I believe that in a few years, Guizhou can become one of the richest provinces in China, and the people of Guizhou can become a model people in China. The ancients said, "Seek more blessings for yourself" and "It is up to people to make things happen." I hope that all the fellow countrymen and comrades in Guizhou can work together to achieve this goal. The meaning that the brothers have contributed to everyone today is roughly these few points. In the future, I hope that everyone can often meet and tell me anything at any time. At the same time, the brothers can also often contribute their ideas to everyone, and discuss and study with each other to achieve the goal of relieving the suffering of the people and building a new Guizhou and a new China. I hope that everyone will work together in this spirit to complete everyone's mission. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Yin Tong Passes Through Nanjing to Visit Huang Fu in Mogan Mountain 11

(Nanjing) Yin Tong arrived in Nanjing at 8:00 AM on the 6th by express train from Tianjin and rested at the Bank of China. According to Yin, he came south this time to visit Huang Fu and others to report on various issues in the war zone and the progress of negotiations, as well as the affairs of the Beining Railway. He will stay in various places for about two weeks before returning to Tianjin. Today, he will take a car to Mogan Mountain to visit Huang and report on everything and ask for instructions. He will arrive in the afternoon and stay for about three days before coming down the mountain to Nanjing. Someone asked Yin whether Huang Fu would accompany him down the mountain. Yin replied that they might come down together. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

(Nanjing) Yin Tong took a car from Nanjing to Mogan Mountain to visit Huang Fu at 10:30 AM on the 6th. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

(Nanjing) Yin Tong, Director of the Beining Railway Bureau, went south from Tianjin on the 4th because the principles for various adjustments in the war zone had been decided by our side. He arrived at Pukou on the morning of the 6th to cross the river and rested at the Central Hotel. He then went to Mogan Mountain via the Nanjing-Hangzhou Highway at 10:30 AM to report to Huang Fu, the Chairman of the Pingzheng Committee. Yin said that the minor issues in the North China war zone had come to an end and that the issue of newly organized security forces entering the war zone to replace defenses would be realized in a short time. This trip to the south was to report on the handling of the war zone and the affairs of the Beining Railway. He will go to Mogan Mountain today to meet with Chairman Huang and, after a delay of three or four days, will accompany Huang from Hangzhou to Shanghai. He will then report on railway affairs to Minister Gu in Shanghai and then come to Nanjing to report everything to President Wang. (Special dispatch, 6th)

Luanyu Area Will Convene an Administrative Meeting 12

(Beiping) The Luanyu District Office plans to convene an administrative meeting after the newly organized security forces in the district enter the war zone and complete the defense replacement by the end of this month or the beginning of next month. The county magistrates and the commanders of the newly organized security forces will attend to discuss local security issues. Because the newly organized security forces in the war zone will enter the war zone in the middle of this month, the Japanese Kwantung Army is using the excuse of protecting overseas Chinese to impose martial law along the Beining Railway. The Kwantung Army headquarters will send two people to enter the pass to monitor the defense replacement of the security forces. (Special dispatch, 6th)

Wang Bingxiao's Troops and the Militia Voluntarily Disband 13

(Beiping) Wang Bingxiao of Yutian has voluntarily disbanded his subordinate militia this morning. Zhao Congyi, the magistrate of Yutian County, telegraphed the Hebei Provincial Government and the Jimi District Office this morning to report. (Special dispatch, 6th)

(Tianjin) The Hebei Provincial Government received a telegram from the Yutian County Government on the 6th reporting that Wang Bingxiao's militia in Yutian County had voluntarily disbanded on the 5th because order in the county had been restored and there was no need to organize a militia. Zhou Yuying's security forces assisted the Yutian County Government in implementing rural cleansing and conducted cleansing operations on various illegal organizations according to regulations. (Special dispatch, 6th)

Hebei Province and Tianjin City Hold Tree Planting Ceremonies 14

(Tianjin) This morning at 10:00 AM, the Hebei Provincial Government held a tree planting ceremony at the First Agricultural Experiment Field at the Tianjin-Pukou Railway West Station. Over 600 leaders from various agencies and circles participated. Chairman Yu Xuezhong and Director Hu Yuanhui of the Department of Construction spoke about the forestry situation in the province, and Xiang Fan of the Tianjin Municipal Party Committee spoke about the significance of the tree planting campaign. They took a photo at 11:00 AM and dispersed. (Special dispatch, 6th)

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Municipal Government planted trees at the Hebei Provincial Stadium this morning at 10:00 AM. Over 300 representatives from various circles attended. Mayor Zhang Ting'e presided over the meeting, and the meeting adjourned at 11:00 AM. (Special dispatch, 6th)

The Ministry of Finance Plans to Draft an Income Tax Law 15

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance is planning to collect income tax. Key personnel of the Tax Department and tax commissioners held a meeting on the 6th to discuss drafting an income tax law for the Legislative Yuan's reference. The scope of collection and the tax rate, after implementation, are estimated to bring in tens of millions of yuan annually. The Ministry is currently planning, and the Legislative Yuan has already started drafting the tax law. The Ministry is also drafting a draft for reference. If time permits, it may be tried out in the second half of the year; otherwise, it will be implemented next year. (Special dispatch, 6th)

The Ministry of Justice Revises and Promulgates the Rules on Time Limits for Criminal Litigation; Effective July 1st 16

(Nanjing) In view of the delays in criminal cases, which cause the parties to suffer years of delays, and at the same time feeling that the current rules on time limits for criminal litigation are not only too lenient but also amended and promulgated during the Beiyang government era and are not in line with the current Criminal Procedure Law, the Ministry of Justice has revised the rules to expedite criminal cases, totaling thirteen articles, and promulgated them on the 6th, effective July 1st. The time limits for criminal trials set in the newly revised rules are divided into six items, except for those following summary procedures: (1) Investigation period: 10 days, the same for rejection or disposition of reconsideration requests; (2) Trial period: 22 days, the same for judgments according to the Provisional Regulations on Review; (3) Judgment period without oral arguments in the first and second instance: 10 days; (4) Time limit for rulings ending the case: 10 days; (5) Time limit for rulings on appeals and further appeals: 7 days, 15 days if facts need to be investigated; (6) Time limit for prosecutors to submit written reasons, defenses, and opinions: 7 days for appeals, 3 days for replies to consultations, and according to Article 2 of the Provisional Regulations on Review for reviews. For complicated or complex cases where the situation cannot be concluded within the time limits in the first two items above, a request may be made to the competent superior for a one-time extension, but it cannot exceed the original time limit. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Yu Youren Summons Inspectors to Beijing 17

(Nanjing) Yu Youren has telegraphed inspectors inside and outside Beijing to come to Beijing immediately to discuss how to proceed. The office for each inspector was originally intended to be an administrative office, but now it has been decided to change it to an office. Each office will be established in an appropriate location within its designated area, not limited to the provincial capital. Each office may have two nominal secretaries and three or four appointed staff members and clerks. In the future, the inspectors will exercise their powers in close coordination. The methods of coordination are currently being drafted. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Fujian Chamber of Commerce Discusses Financial Relief 18

(Fuzhou) Due to the financial depletion in the market, the Provincial Chamber of Commerce convened an emergency meeting to discuss methods of adjustment. President Luo Mianhou and others made a request for relief to the provincial government and sent a letter to the Shanghai Bank of China asking it to still set up a branch in Fuzhou to issue banknotes, and for Qian Zhuang to be able to use real estate as collateral for loans. The provincial government has agreed to transfer one million yuan from the provincial banking sector specifically for commercial circulation. (Special dispatch, 6th)

French Ambassador Meets Xu Mo at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs 19

(Nanjing) French Ambassador Weilitun went to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the morning of the 6th to meet with Vice Minister Xu Mo. It is said that they discussed outstanding issues between China and France. He left after an hour. (Special dispatch, 6th)

Japanese Consuls from Various Places Pass Through Nanjing to Shanghai 20

(Nanjing) Wakisaka, the secretary of the Japanese embassy in Beiping, Sakane, the Japanese consul in Qingdao, Kawagoe, the Japanese consul in Tianjin, and Nishida, the Japanese consul in Jinan, passed through Nanjing on the Beiping-Shanghai through train at 9:00 PM on the evening of the 6th to Shanghai. Miura, the Japanese consul in Hankou, also passed through Nanjing to Shanghai on the Nanyang Maru on the afternoon of the 6th to attend the consul conference convened by the Japanese ambassador in Shanghai. (Special dispatch, 6th)

(Xiamen) Tsukamoto, the Japanese consul in Xiamen, went to Shanghai on the Taiyuan Wheel on the 5th to attend the conference of consuls in China held in Shanghai on the 8th before Arichi's return to his country. (Special dispatch, 6th)

The Ministry of Railways Forms Economic Survey Teams for Shaanxi and Gansu 21

(Nanjing) There are concrete plans for the extension of the Longhai Railway from Xi'an to the Xilan section. In order to understand this situation, the Ministry of Railways has decided to first form two economic survey teams to go to various places in Shaanxi and Gansu Provinces to conduct on-the-spot surveys. They are expected to be formed in the middle of this month and will depart from Beijing. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

All Members of the Control Yuan Commemorate Gao Youshan 22

(Nanjing) The memorial service for the late Control Committee member Gao Youtang was held at the First Park on the afternoon of the 6th. Because the President of the Yuan was unable to attend due to other business, Vice President Ding Weifen presided over the ceremony. After the ceremony, Control Committee member Yang Ruo reported on Gao's life, followed by thanks from Gao's family. (Special dispatch, 6th)

Several hundred people attended, including Ding Weifen, Wang Luyi, Chen Zhishuo, and all the Control Committee members. Ding Weifen presided over the ceremony, and all the Control Committee members accompanied the ceremony. Control Committee member Yang Tianji then reported on Gao Youtang's life. The atmosphere at the meeting was exceptionally solemn. Afterwards, the family members expressed their gratitude, and a photo was taken before dispersing. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Current Affairs Commentary

U.S. Amendment Proposal on Silver and the Future of China's Monetary System 24

— Ren

In the recent six years, the overseas silver market has been unstable. Prices rise and fall rapidly, changing in an instant. China, being on the silver standard, bears the brunt of these changes. Consequently, the value of our currency fluctuates accordingly, and our economy and society experience periods of both advancement and setback. Recalling the times when gold was expensive and silver was cheap, the people of the nation were filled with anxiety, fearing that cheap silver would result in "pound losses" in finance and excessively high "settlement prices" in trade, causing numerous harms. Therefore, some people called for banning the import of silver, while others called for prohibiting speculation in silver. Observing the recent situation of expensive silver and cheap gold, the people of the nation are once again filled with anxiety, fearing that expensive silver will lead to stagnant exports and increased import surpluses, resulting in only harms and no benefits. Consequently, some call for banning the export of silver, while others call for prohibiting speculative trading. Thus, if the price of silver remains unchanged, it is fine. But if there are drastic changes, whether rising or falling, it will inevitably cause the people of the nation to be filled with anxiety.

According to American telegrams, Senator McCarran of the U.S. Senate has proposed abolishing three clauses of the Silver Purchase Act: (1) nationalization of silver; (2) management or restriction of silver trading; and (3) taxation of 50% on silver surpluses. Although this proposal is opposed by the silver faction and may not pass, it shows that the progress of Roosevelt's silver policy may not be entirely smooth. However, if this proposal were to pass, it would be tantamount to declaring a flaw in Roosevelt's policy, and the world silver market would surely experience another major upheaval. If so, one wave subsides, and another rises, wouldn't this again cause the people of the nation to be filled with anxiety?

China's currency panics along with silver prices, causing economic and social instability. On the surface, it seems that the reason for this is the use of silver as the monetary standard. Therefore, some modern people believe that replacing silver with paper, or replacing silver with gold, or replacing silver with a "capacity standard" would solve the monetary panic of recent years and stabilize China's economy and society. However, if we examine the essence of currency, it is not something that comes with the birth of mankind. Before indirect exchange in the past, there was no such thing as currency. If the system of indirect exchange in human society were to disappear in the future, currency would also disappear with it. In the continuous history of mankind, currency can only exist in indirect exchange societies because it is a medium of exchange, only needed under the indirect exchange system. As for the evolution of monetary materials from ordinary goods (such as the earliest shell money in China) to metals and then to paper money, it is due to the evolution of economic society. Therefore, the evolution of society is the cause, and the change in currency is the effect. If one wants to force social evolution by changing monetary materials, it is tantamount to reversing cause and effect. This is definitely impossible.

Today, China's economy and society are characterized by extremely backward production and unsound distribution. Thus, any external change causes unrest. The rise and fall of silver prices in recent years is one such external change. If we ask whether the rise or fall of silver prices is beneficial or harmful to China's economy, the answer must be that a rise in silver prices is harmful to China, and a fall in silver prices is also harmful to China. From this, it can be seen that changes in silver prices are merely a contributing factor, and the reason why this contributing factor can trigger a crisis of panic lies in the fundamental unsoundness of China's economic organization. It is like a firecracker containing gunpowder, which can explode when lit with a fuse or with a match. The fuse and the match are both contributing factors. If one wants to prevent the firecracker from exploding at all, one must first remove the gunpowder, which is the gene for explosion. There is no better strategy than this. This principle is very clear and needs no further explanation.

From the above discussion, it is clear that currency is merely a product of society, and that changes in currency are premised on the evolution of exchange society. The root cause of the current economic and social stagnation in China does not seem to lie in currency. If the fundamental defects in our national economy today are not eliminated, then even if we replace the current silver standard with gold, paper, or "capacity," it would not be of much help. It may even cause general unease in society due to the change in the monetary system and the fluctuation of currency values. Therefore, when discussing China's monetary system today from the essence of currency, I believe that it is necessary to maintain the unified monetary system that China has already achieved. While maintaining a part of the already unified monetary system, one should seek the independence of the national economy with the fastest and most effective strategies. Then, China's economy and society will naturally gradually move onto the path of evolution. If the economy and society can indeed thrive and move forward along the path of evolution, then there is no need to worry about the monetary system not being able to improve. Therefore, whether China's monetary system can be improved or not, the fundamental key lies not in forcing the reform of monetary materials, nor in whether the proposed U.S. amendment on silver can become a reality, but rather in whether the defects in China's economic society itself can be eliminated. This is something that the people of the nation should clearly understand.

Three-Nation Conference to Open Soon: Italian Premier Drafts Plan; Three-Nation Representatives to First Discuss Procedures in London; Eden Returns to England, Says Crisis Can Be Remedied 25

(Rome) The Stresa Conference of England, France, and Italy is scheduled to open on Thursday. Italian Premier Mussolini today took his private plane to Villa Folli to draft a concrete plan to be proposed at the meeting. It is reported that Mussolini wants the three nations to discuss a practical action plan, the main purpose of which is to consider the overall situation caused by Germany's rearmament. Italy's view is that the main difficulty at present is to comply with Germany's demands on armaments while preventing Germany from encroaching on Austria's independence. Italy was greatly alarmed after Germany announced the reintroduction of compulsory military service and recently ordered the recall of reserve soldiers from 1912 for readiness. (Reuters, 5th)

(Rome) Premier Mussolini today piloted a three-engine plane, flying over the Apennine Mountains at an altitude of 6,000 meters, and landed safely at the Folli airfield. He then drove to his villa in Comminate. Mussolini often goes to his former residence near Folli for a few days of rest before state affairs meetings. This time it is in preparation for the Stresa Conference. The Stresa conference venue is being arranged. Hundreds of gendarmes and craftsmen are currently busy cleaning the Palazzo Borromeo on Isola Bella. Mussolini will reside in the Napoleon Room or the Empress Josephine Room when attending the conference. (National Telegram, 5th)

(London) Representatives of England, France, and Italy will hold talks here on the procedures for the Stresa Conference on April 11. They will probably first discuss the British report on the results of Simon's visit to Germany and Eden's visit to Russia, Poland, and Czechoslovakia. Whether the names of the British representatives participating in the Stresa Conference will be announced in the House of Commons on Monday has not yet been decided by British Prime Minister MacDonald. (Reuters, 6th)

Eden Returns to England and Makes a Statement

(London) Eden arrived at Victoria Station at 8:43 tonight, looking very tired. His wife and Foreign Secretary Simon were at the station to greet him. Eden told reporters that his trip to five capitals, including Paris, Berlin, Moscow, Warsaw, and Prague, was overwhelming but beneficial. The difficulties of the European situation are indeed great, but they are not irremediable. If these difficulties are to be overcome, then all countries must fulfill their due obligations. Britain will pursue its sincere, resolute, and courageous foreign policy and support the League of Nations and collective peace. The opinions of the governments he heard during his talks with the authorities in the five capitals are now being carefully studied by the relevant departments of the British government.

Eden and Simon will attend a cabinet meeting on Monday to submit a report. Simon will then address the House of Commons the following day. The general public is now eagerly awaiting this because Simon and Eden will be traveling to Italy to participate in the Stresa Conference on Tuesday. The conference is scheduled to open on April 11. After the conference, Simon and Eden will travel to Geneva because the League of Nations Council has scheduled a special meeting for April 15 to consider Germany's rearmament. Whether Prime Minister MacDonald will accompany Simon and Eden to Stresa is not yet known. (Reuters, 5th)

Key Points of the Three-Nation Conference Agenda

(London) The British Foreign Office today received the agenda for the upcoming Stresa Conference from Italian Premier Mussolini, which contains the following four points: (1) England, France, and Italy will decide on a common policy regarding Germany's rearmament; (2) They will decide on a common strategy for the three nations when the League of Nations Council meets; (3) They will discuss Austria's independence and plan to protect Austria's integrity; and (4) They will study the possibility of revising the peace treaties of Hungary, Austria, and Bulgaria. The Italian Premier also expressed a strong desire to conclude an air force mutual assistance pact with France and England. France and Italy will firmly oppose a German-Austrian alliance, and Britain also holds the same view. British Prime Minister MacDonald, French Premier Flandin, and Italian Premier Mussolini will represent their respective governments at the Stresa Conference. In addition, British Foreign Secretary Simon and Lord Privy Seal Eden will also attend. Austria has already indicated that it will send one representative to participate in the conference. The Schuschnigg government plans to request that the existing army of 30,000 be doubled and that conscription be restored. The Austrian Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Walden are now very friendly to France and oppose the policies of German leader Hitler. However, it is reported that Austrian public opinion tends toward a German-Austrian alliance. If the current government concludes an alliance with other countries, it will not be able to maintain its position. Mussolini denied the rumor that Germany would participate in the conference but did not comment on whether the Nazi government should be invited to participate. The Italian newspaper "Forum" recently suggested that if an understanding with Germany is desired, England, France, and Italy must first establish an agreement to exclude Germany. Diplomatic circles believe that Italian Premier Mussolini will act on this suggestion and genuinely join hands with England and France to oppose Germany's rearmament. The British government is still studying the memorandum submitted by Germany during Foreign Secretary Simon's visit to Berlin. It is reported that Hitler made several suggestions in the memorandum, such as (1) concluding an international convention prohibiting economic and financial assistance to any aggressor; (2) a ten-year truce; and (3) signing a treaty similar to the Kellogg-Briand Pact. Officials claim that using this plan to replace the Eastern European Security Pact is like going backward. (Reuters, 6th)

Pay Attention to Guaranteeing Austria's Independence

(Paris) French Foreign Minister Laval will submit a memorandum at the Stresa Conference explaining the reasons why the French government is appealing to the League of Nations Council against Germany's violation of the Treaty of Versailles by reintroducing compulsory military service. The League of Nations Council has scheduled a meeting for April 16 to discuss the resolution on Germany's rearmament. Laval will then submit a draft resolution. Paris now hopes that England, France, and Italy will jointly submit this proposal. It is reported that the Italian government recently inquired about the following matters: (1) the opinions of the French and British governments regarding the future meeting of the League of Nations Council; (2) the organization of collective security; and (3) the maintenance of Austria's independence. It is now believed that the rearmament of small European countries has also been mentioned. Paris, like Rome, is now paying close attention to the issue of guaranteeing Austria's independence. However, it believes that the military clauses of the revised treaties between the Allied Powers and Austria and Hungary must first be agreed upon by the Little Entente (Czechoslovakia, Romania, Yugoslavia). It is reported that the French government plans to propose a Europe-wide plan based on the hope of obtaining the agreement of England, Italy, Germany, and Russia. (Reuters, 5th)

Secretary of War Declares Peaceful Aspirations

(London) Secretary of War Lord Hailsham recently issued a statement, pointing out Britain's desire to maintain peace and expressing deep concern that Britain's national power is too weak to suit the current international situation. Hailsham said that no one in continental Europe fears Britain's armaments, nor does anyone believe that Britain's armaments are a threat to peace. On the contrary, Britain's military installations are specifically designed to safeguard peace. He then mentioned the visits of Simon, Eden, and others to Germany, Russia, Poland, and Czechoslovakia, saying that no country other than Britain could make such a trip and succeed. (Havas, 6th)

To Be Discussed at Next Week's Cabinet Meeting

(Paris) The Council of State met this morning and approved the resolution of yesterday's Supreme National Defense Committee, stipulating that the recruits who were to be discharged on April 13 this year should continue to stay in camp for training for at least three months. The Council of State then decided to hold an extraordinary cabinet meeting next Tuesday to review the issues to be raised at the Stresa Conference and the extraordinary meeting of the League of Nations Council. Finally, Commerce Minister Marchandeau explained the Franco-Belgian commercial agreement concluded yesterday in the Belgian capital, which was approved by the Council of State. (Havas, 6th)

French Newspapers Observe Britain's Softening Stance

(Paris) The newspapers here all want to understand what attitude Britain will take at the Stresa Conference. Italy's attitude is quite consistent with France's and is already very clear. French newspapers hope that Britain will also adopt the same clear attitude as Italy. "Le Petit Parisien" said, "Italian Premier Mussolini firmly advocates that the Stresa Conference should achieve positive results. Compared to Britain's efforts to advocate limiting the purpose of the conference to merely exchanging opinions, this advocacy of the Italian Premier is especially commendable. As for the softening of Britain's attitude, if we explore the reason, it is actually due to its domestic political situation, not the result of inquiries in Berlin." "Paris Echo" said that a solution aimed at establishing a new European convention is actually a self-deceiving trick, which is only enough to expose the weakness and incompetence of various countries. The great powers cannot effectively resist Germany, so they are using this to cover up. "White Paper" pointed out that the opinions of England and Italy are diametrically opposed, saying, "Italy's position is clear and definite and does not need to be repeated, and there is no need to doubt where we should go." "Le Petit Journal" said, "Although direct consultations between England, France, and Italy on April 11 are necessary, it would be too arbitrary to say that England, France, and Italy must reach an agreement immediately." (Havas, 6th)

British Newspapers Comment on European Peace

(London) "The Daily Telegraph" commented on the statement issued by Lord Privy Seal Eden, saying that the following conclusions can be drawn: (1) The European situation is indeed very tense, but a serious conflict will not occur as quickly as generally expected; (2) Poland's opposition to the collective security system is not impossible to overcome, and Germany's attitude may not remain so rigid; (3) The countries visited have no aggressive ambitions and are willing to organize peace institutions; (4) Britain's policy is based on organizing peace institutions. If it can continue to implement a sincere, strong, and courageous policy, it will surely help Europe achieve its peace goals. "The News Chronicle" stated that Eden's trip could have the following diplomatic effects: (1) Various countries have greater trust in Eden; (2) Public confidence in regional conventions has greatly decreased. Germany and Poland do not believe that the Eastern European Pact is beneficial. This plan has now died. As for the Danube Pact, which maintains Austria's independence, it is on its deathbed because German Premier Hitler insists that the Austrian people should have the right to clearly express their will regarding their future destiny (referring to holding a referendum). In addition, the Locarno Treaty, although still in existence, produces a very small sense of security because France and Germany have close relations with Eastern European countries. Once a war breaks out in Eastern Europe, these countries will inevitably be drawn into the vortex. In short, European countries must quickly choose between a collective security system and a chaotic situation. Therefore, the international talks in the coming half-month are of great importance to peace and war. Since the establishment of the Treaty of Versailles, there has been no impact as great as this. (Havas, 6th)

Monetary Tides in Europe: France and Belgium Discuss and Plan Agreement; Dutch and Swiss Currencies Sold Off in London Market; Netherlands Denies Abandoning Gold Standard 26

Brussels A delegation from the French Ministry of Commerce previously came here to study the impact of the devaluation of the Belgian currency on Franco-Belgian trade. An agreement has now been drafted, stipulating that goods imported from Belgium into France will maintain the same prices as the world market, and France will abandon its plan to increase special surtaxes on these goods. Belgian officials and business circles were greatly relieved to hear this news, because they were deeply afraid that the protective tariffs adopted by France would render Belgium's devaluation plan useless. (National Telegram, 6th)

(Paris) French Premier Flandin told the French trade union today that there is little hope of immediately stopping the international currency war, but the convening of an international conference has already been launched. However, the opposition of other countries has greatly undermined the hope of currency stability. The French Premier reiterated that France will maintain the gold standard regardless of the actions of other countries, but international currency stability is greatly beneficial to all countries. (National Telegram, 6th)

Brussels, Belgian Capital After talks between Belgian Premier Zeeland and French Commerce Minister Marchandeau, the following communiqué was issued: "The French and Belgian cabinet members conducted talks in an atmosphere of sincerity and mutual trust. The cabinet members of the two countries believe that the changes in the monetary systems of Belgium and Luxembourg will lower prices and affect trade between the three countries. Efforts should now be made to avoid these effects. This is the common view of France and Belgium. For this reason, the cabinet members of the two countries have drafted an agreement that will be sent to the governments of France, Belgium, and Luxembourg tomorrow for joint approval." (Havas, 5th)

(London) In the London foreign exchange market today, the Dutch and Swiss currencies were sold off in large quantities, and British pounds were purchased, leading to an increase in the pound's value. Although the rumor from Paris that the Netherlands refused to sell gold was denied, the sale of the Dutch currency continued unabated. People in Paris believe that the Netherlands has now abandoned the gold standard in real terms because the value of the Dutch currency is far below the gold export point. They also believe that the British authorities' failure to use their equalization fund to prevent the rise of the British pound shows that the British authorities are confident that both the Netherlands and Switzerland will soon abandon the gold standard. According to reliable sources in Amsterdam, the anxiety about the devaluation of the Dutch currency is completely unfounded. There is no reason for the panic in Paris that the Dutch bank is not selling gold. The Netherlands has not refused to ship gold to France. The Dutch bank usually does not release gold in the afternoon and will still have to release it the next morning. It is expected that the Dutch bank's interest rate will increase by one percent tonight in order to prevent attacks by speculative investors. It is estimated that the Dutch bank lost a total of 4,000 gold florins worth of gold to the United States and France today. (Reuters, 5th)

The Hague, Dutch Capital This afternoon, speculators continued to attack the Dutch currency. It is now reported that the Dutch National Bank will raise the discount rate to 4.5 percent tonight in order to resist the attacks. According to some estimates, the Dutch National Bank's gold reserves have shipped 40 million guilders abroad today. The Dutch National Bank once suspended the release of cash this afternoon, which caused various rumors. In fact, this is a common practice. According to responsible sources in the National Bank, the National Bank's policy on the gold standard issue has not changed. The rumors of currency devaluation are completely unfounded. (Havas, 5th)

Armed Peace: French Troops Deployed to German Border; Discharged Recruits to Stay in Camp for Training; Austrian Arms Factory Prepares to Start Work 27

(Paris) France today continued to send three military groups to the German border. According to official announcements, all troops will be stationed at defensive projects made of steel and cement between Germany and France. From Belgium to Switzerland, the French army is busy mobilizing, traveling by car, train, or on foot, one after another on the way, reminiscent of the scenes of the European War. Other preparations are also underway. (National Telegram, 6th)

(Paris) The Supreme National Defense Committee met this afternoon, attended by Premier Flandin, Foreign Minister Laval, Navy Minister Pietri, Army Minister Maurin, Aviation Minister Trélat, General Pétain, Army Chief of Staff Gamelin, and Navy Chief of Staff Darlan. It is reported that today's meeting decided that the recruits who were to be discharged on April 13 this year should continue to stay in camp for training for at least three months. This resolution must be approved by the Council of State tomorrow morning before it can be finalized. (Havas, 5th)

Vienna The Vienna Arms Factory, which has been abandoned for a long time, was ordered today to relocate its 700 resident families in preparation for starting work. This shows that Austria has taken a further step in seeking to restore its armaments. The factory is full of military supplies, but it has not been used since the Treaty of Saint-Germain was signed. (National Telegram, 5th)

Danzig Parliament Election: Hitler's Representative's Campaign Speech, British Newspapers Comment that Germany is Humiliating Others 28

Election Forecast (Geneva) The Free City of Danzig will hold elections for new parliamentary members tomorrow. All parties related to the League of Nations expect the National Socialist Party to win 80% of the vote. The National Socialist Party must obtain a two-thirds majority to petition the League of Nations to amend the city's constitution. The matter is almost predetermined. If the National Socialist Party does obtain a majority, the Senate will attempt to amend the constitution, but doing so without the League of Nations' consent would be illegal, and the League is unlikely to agree. This is the opinion of well-informed sources. Should this situation arise, Germany will not be prepared to resist the League of Nations with a fait accompli. According to the Danzig constitution, the parliament has 72 members, elected every four years. There is also a Senate, with a president, vice-president, and ten senators. The Senate is the highest state authority, elected by the parliament for an indefinite term. The parliament can amend the constitution by a two-thirds majority, provided that at least two-thirds of the members are present. (Reuters, 6th)

Polish Indignation Warsaw Polish political circles are greatly indignant about the National Socialist Party's election campaign in Danzig. Prussian Prime Minister General Göring recently stated in a speech to the public in Danzig that Danzig is German. This reveals the "annexationist aim." The Polish Deputy Foreign Minister stated in a speech today that as long as the Vistula River flows as it does today, Danzig will never change.

Free City of Danzig Hitler's representative, Hess, delivered a speech at a rally in Zappot today, praising the National Socialist Party and urging the public to participate in Sunday's election. Hess made a lengthy statement on the international political situation, saying that the Berlin authorities were very angry about the death sentences and imprisonment of German nationals in Memel. Although British lawyers had argued against it, they had not been able to secure their release. Hess also said that Germany's continued tolerance of this matter proves Germany's efforts for peace, which would probably not be the case for Britain, France, and Italy. Germany is deeply concerned that intervention would disrupt the peace of Europe. It is up to the powerful countries who claim to guarantee the region to correct this. (National Telegram, 6th)

Warsaw The Free City of Danzig will hold elections on April 7. Prussian Governor Göring went to Danzig to attend the National Socialist Party's election conference and delivered a speech, stating, "Germany is determined not to retake the Free City of Danzig by force. However, it is very clear that the people of Danzig are leaning towards Germany, so Danzig will sooner or later be merged into Germany." Göring also said, "Germany is prepared to join hands with its neighbor France. If France genuinely desires peace, then Foreign Minister Laval need not travel all the way to Moscow. Wouldn't it be better to change course and visit Berlin?" Finally, he hoped that the people of Danzig would fulfill their civic duty this Sunday by voting for the National Socialist Party, because supporting the National Socialist Party means supporting Germany. (Havas, 5th)

(London) The Times commented on the current situation in Memel and Danzig, saying that the German National Socialist Party is being humiliated by others in the Memel region, but wants to humiliate others in Danzig. The greatest difficulty Lithuania has in maintaining relations with Germany is the issue of Memel's autonomy, which Lithuania is not happy to hear. If Germany's radio propaganda to overseas Chinese were not so exaggerated, then the Lithuanian government's punishment of the National Socialist Party members in the Memel region and its assimilation policy would not be so severe. (Havas, 6th)

Page 7

US to Convene Silver Conference, Lynck Proposes Resolution to Organize Special Committee, to Study Silver Purchase Plan to Ensure No Doubt in Sino-US Relations 29

(Washington) The silver faction held a meeting here today and passed a resolution to organize a special committee to study the impact of the silver purchase plan on Sino-US relations. The proposer was Lynck, advisor to the Chinese government. The meeting was hosted by the American Silver Association and will last for two days. (National Telegram, 5th)

(Washington) At the Silver Conference convened by the National Silver Industry Federation, Democratic Congressman Dies stated that the United States is now in a position to force the world to adopt bimetallism. The United States should immediately restore silver coinage to raise domestic prices and stabilize global currency. Congressional silver faction members all participated in the meeting. Chairman Allen delivered an opening speech, advocating for greater understanding of silver and its uses, saying that silver is a difficult problem for the United States, but if properly addressed, it could provide jobs for tens of thousands of people and benefit the entire country. Allen advocated increasing the price of silver to $1.29 per ounce. Lynck, legal advisor to the Chinese government, advocated for greater use of silver as a way to solve unemployment and other problems, and advocated for increasing trade between China and the United States based on pure commodity exchange methods. Thomas and others were elected as members of the resolution review committee and will report on ways to increase the price of silver tomorrow. (Reuters, 5th)

Female Writer: Sudden Death of Two German Women, Investigation Confirms Suicide, Attempted to Rescue Abducted Reporter 30

(London) London police now believe that the remains of two German women (one, Dr. Fabian, 36, a socialist writer, and the other, the wife of the late German civil servant Wim, also a writer, 56) found in a locked room in a house in London on Thursday died by suicide. Rumors that they were murdered by secret agents of the German government are untrue. The cause of their death was likely due to their anxiety about not receiving renewed permission from the British authorities to reside in London, fearing they would be forced to return to Germany. The two women had recently been in contact with Dr. Weismann to try to rescue German anti-National Socialist journalist Jakobi, who was kidnapped from Switzerland into Germany by National Socialist Party members. Dr. Weismann admitted to being involved in the kidnapping, which caused friction between Switzerland and Germany. The British House of Commons paid close attention to the unexplained deaths of the two German women, and a member of parliament questioned the matter yesterday. (Reuters, 6th)

(London) Two female friends of German journalist Jakobi, who was kidnapped in Switzerland by the German National Socialist Party, lived in an apartment in Bloomsbury, London. One was Dr. Fabian, a German socialist writer, and the other was Mrs. Wim, also a writer. Both died suddenly in their apartment yesterday. The cause is unknown, which caused considerable surprise to the general public. A member of the British House of Commons even raised questions about this matter. The detective team has now found out that the two women did commit suicide, because the period of their residence in Britain was due to expire next month and could not be extended. They were deeply afraid of being oppressed by the National Socialist Party if they returned to Germany, so they committed suicide. According to friends of the two women, a suicide note has been found in their residence, proving that it was suicide. (Havas, 5th)

(London) The police have completed the investigation into the sudden death of the two German women. It is said that when the inquest court opens on April 10, the authorities will present evidence to prove that the death of the two women was caused by despair and suicide, and there was no political relationship. (Reuters, 6th)

Japan Decides to Revise Russo-Japanese Fisheries Treaty, Has Telegraphed Japanese Ambassador to Russia to Negotiate 32

Soviet Russian Balloon Ascends into Stratosphere, Reaching a Record Height of 24.5 Miles, Equipped with an Electrical Man That Automatically Sends Signals 33

(Moscow) A Soviet Russian balloon ascended into the stratosphere today, reaching a height of over 24.5 miles, more than doubling the American record. This flight was of great value and contributed greatly to science. The balloon did not have anyone inside, but was equipped with an electrical man that automatically sent various signals about the ascent. Many Soviet scientists received reports of temperature changes as the balloon reached areas beyond human reach in the radio room here. According to these signals, the balloon's speed was 15 miles per hour. The lowest temperature was -76 degrees Celsius when the balloon reached an altitude of 30,000 feet. The balloon reached 130,000 feet, or over 24.5 miles, far exceeding the height of 61,236 feet reached by the American Settle and others in 1933. In recent years, there have been repeated attempts to ascend into the stratosphere, the main purpose of which is to study the guiding trend of cosmic rays. However, the famous atmospheric world aviator Post recently made an attempt to pass through the stratosphere from Los Angeles to New York to test whether the upper atmosphere can be a medium for regular commercial flights. (Reuters, 5th)

US Congressmen Propose Strict Neutrality Bill, Political Figures Express Dissatisfaction, Equivalent to Rewarding Aggressor Nations 34

(Washington) Congressmen intend to maintain the United States' neutral position in the event of a European war and want to stipulate a clear policy by law. Many bills have been proposed, with claims such as (1) Regardless of right or wrong, all warring countries are prohibited from supplying arms or providing loans; (2) The principle of freedom of the seas is abandoned. Any American merchant who trades with warring countries is deemed to be at fault if they encounter obstacles. Also, government offices may refuse to issue passports to Americans who travel to dangerous areas during wartime. Some political figures expressed dissatisfaction with this kind of bill, saying that it goes beyond the scope. If the United States does not distinguish between warring countries and considers maintaining neutrality as its ability, then aggression cannot be prevented, and the invaded country is more likely to fail without support, which is equivalent to punishing peaceful nations and rewarding aggressor nations. (Havas, 5th)

We hope that all sectors of the Japanese financial community will assist our research work and provide various useful materials. After inspecting Japan, we will continue to inspect China and the Philippines. Although the increase in Japan-US trade relations depends on the power of the government, the increase in friendly relations between the two countries is a prerequisite. Greco-Albanian Dispute, Hague Court Announces Verdict, Greek Minority Wins 37

The Hague In Albania, there is a Greek minority, whose language, religion, and ethnicity are different from the natives. The Albanian government issued a declaration to the Administrative Council of the League of Nations in December 1921, allowing minorities in the country to establish their own religious charity organizations and schools, and to freely use their language and writing. Later, Albania promulgated a law in 1933, nationalizing all schools in the country and prohibiting minorities from running their own schools, which was opposed by the Greek government and submitted to the Hague Permanent Court of International Justice for trial last month. Albania and Greece sent representatives to court to defend their cases. The International Court of Justice has now announced its verdict by a vote of eight to three. The Greek side won the case. The verdict stated that "Albanian citizens whose ethnicity, religion, and language belong to a minority have the right to use their own funds to maintain, operate, manage, and establish various charitable religious social organizations and schools, and to freely use their national language and freely practice their religious rituals." (Havas, 6th)

US President's Public Works Bill, Passage Through Both Houses Imminent 38

(Washington) President Roosevelt's $4.88 billion public works relief bill, the purpose of which is to establish public works projects to employ millions of unemployed people at lower wages than in private industries, is expected to become law within a few days. The report of the joint committee of both houses on this bill has been passed by both the Senate and the House of Representatives today and is now sent to the President for signature and implementation. The final form of this bill is in line with President Roosevelt's wishes, stipulating a maximum wage of $50. (Reuters, 5th)

Standards for Appointment of Court Clerks 50

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Justice has formulated six articles of provisional regulations on the standards for the appointment of court clerks, which were promulgated and implemented on the 6th. The positions of clerk are divided into appointed and recommended. Appointed clerks must have passed the general examination for court clerks, or have served in appointed positions in judicial organs and passed screening or performance evaluation, or have served as clerks in the Ministry of Justice or the court for more than three years and have excellent performance, or have graduated from law schools above the specialized level. Recommended clerks must be current or former recommended court clerks who have passed screening or performance evaluation, or have the qualifications of recommended civil servants. (Central News Agency, 6th)

Contents of Various Water Conservancy Regulations 51

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan Committee has drafted organizational regulations for the Yangtze River, Taihu Lake, and North China Water Conservancy Commissions. The Legislative Yuan's Legal System and Economic Committees are in the process of reviewing them. The important contents of the draft are as follows: (1) Each commission is directly under the Executive Yuan Committee and is responsible for all matters related to promoting benefits and eliminating disasters in the Yangtze River, Taihu Lake, and their related lakes and rivers, as well as the Yellow River's northern tributaries flowing into the Bohai Sea and coastal areas. (2) Each commission will have one director-general and a number of selected commissioners appointed by the Executive Yuan Committee. (3) Each commission will have two departments: General Affairs and Engineering. With approval, they may establish surveying teams, hydrological stations, meteorological observatories, engineering offices, and project management offices. They may also hire domestic and foreign water conservancy experts as consultants or special commissioners. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Northwest Inspection Record 80

— Special Correspondent for this Newspaper, Ya

Gansu Province Water Conservancy Eagerly Awaiting Development

Gansu Province is located in the upper reaches of the Yellow River, covering a vast area. However, due to the arid plateau and lack of irrigation resources, as far as the eye can see, the land is barren. If prompt remedies are not sought, not only will there be no resources for national construction, but also the more than 5.6 million people of Gansu Province will constantly experience disasters and be greatly diminished. However, the way to remedy this must first be to open up rivers and canals, repair ditches and waterways, so that high-lying fields can be irrigated in time, turning barren land into fertile land, enriching people's livelihoods and easing national finances. Moreover, it will also be beneficial to the future of the Yellow River management. Therefore, when talking about the development of the Northwest, everyone focuses on water conservancy and transportation. Speaking of Gansu Province, water conservancy is even more important than transportation. Because with developed transportation and backward water conservancy, if there are imported goods being dumped and no products can be transported internally, the rural economy of the province will inevitably fall into a more desperate situation. Now I visited the Director of the Construction Department, Mr. Xu Xianshi, who expressed his opinions on the Gansu Province water conservancy plan, which is quite noteworthy. I specially record it as follows, awaiting the central government's assistance in handling it, or investment and development by capitalists from various provinces.

Gansu is located on a plateau with scarce rainfall. The areas that rely on irrigation are the Yellow River basin, which runs across the middle of the province from west to east. Gaolan, Jingyuan, and Yongjing counties are all situated along the river. The remaining tributaries are distributed in the south of the river, including the Daxia River, which reaches Yongjing, Linxia, and Xiahe counties; the Tao River, which reaches Tao Sha, Lintao, Minxian, Linze, Kangle, Ningding, and Zheng counties; the Xiangshui River, which reaches Yuzhong County; the Zuli River, which reaches Huining and Dingxi counties; and the Qingshui River, which reaches Haiyuan and Guyuan counties. In the north of the river, there is the Datong River, which spans the border between Gansu and Qinghai; the Zhuanglang River, which reaches Yongdeng County. In addition, belonging to Longdong, there is the Huan River, which reaches Huanxian, Qingyang, and Heshui counties; the Malian River, which reaches Ningxian and Zhengning counties; the Dahei River, which reaches Zhenyuan County; and the Jing River, which reaches Jingchuan, Lingtai, Pingliang, Huaping, Chongxin, and Huating counties. Belonging to Longnan, there is the Wei River, which reaches Qingshui, Tianshui, Qin'an, Zhuanglang, Longde, Jingning, Gangu, Tongwei, Wushan, Longxi, Weiyuan, and Zhangxian counties; the Mapaoquan River, which reaches Liangdang County; the Hengchuan River, which reaches Huixian County; the Xiniu River, which reaches Chengxian, Lixian, Kangxian, and Xihe counties; and the Bailong River, which reaches Wudu, Wenxian, and Xigu counties. Belonging to the northwest of Long, there is the Dang River, which reaches Dunhuang County; the Shule River, which reaches Anxi and Yumen counties; the Beida River, which reaches Jinta and Jiuquan counties; and the Hei River, which reaches Dingxin, Gaotai, Linze, Zhangye, Minle, and Shandan counties. The Jinchuan Gorge enters Yongchang County, and the Baita River reaches Minqin, Wuwei, and Gulang counties. In general, only Jingtai County relies solely on the snow on Mao Mao Mountain for irrigation, without large ditches for storage. Other areas, such as the Beihu River, Jinchuan Gorge, and Baita River in the northwest, all rely on the snow accumulation in the Helan Mountains and Qishushan Mountains as their only water source. Therefore, they often dry up after winter. The above is the distribution of the main rivers and canals in Gansu Province. Its tributaries are interwoven, and there is the possibility of opening them up everywhere. Therefore, Gansu water conservancy is not worried about the lack of water sources, but about the difficulty of the project. In the past, most of the water conservancy projects were carried out by local gentry and people within their capabilities, with the government providing assistance, opening up canals and ditches, or setting up waterwheels along the river to benefit one party. There is still no overall plan for the whole province. According to the investigation, the most notable achievement among the completed canals that can be used for整理 calculation is in Lintao County, which has opened up twelve canals, irrigating 57,700 mu of land. Next are the thirty-two counties, including Gaolan, which have opened up 213 canals, irrigating more than 2.6 million mu of land. Yongjing and other four counties have installed waterwheels, totaling 254, irrigating more than 50,000 mu of land. In total, the irrigated farmland that has been solved is about 2.71 million mu. Gansu Province is located on a plateau, and any land that can be irrigated with water can become paddy fields. Therefore, although the number of paddy fields in the province has not been fully investigated, those that can be irrigated and are not worried about drought are mostly like this. There are also three canals in Lintao County, two canals in Tao Sha County, and one canal in Yongdeng County that have been discussed but not yet completed. The total cost of the project is estimated to be more than 42,600 yuan, and it can irrigate more than 39,000 mu of land. Currently, it is planned to open the Minsheng, Anchuan, and Puji canals in Lintao County, the Xingu, Dajiachuan, and Guantan gully canals in Gaolan County, the Tao La Yan Gan River Canal in Wuwei County, the West and South Changning rivers canals in Longxi County, the Heimaquan river canal in Jingtai County, the Honggucheng canal in Yongdeng County, the Pingliangchuan canal in Pingliang County, the Jing and Rui canals in Jingchuan County, the guiding Longhe canal in Tianshui County, and the Kushui, Weirong 鈸, and Xinglong canals in Jingning County. The total cost of the project is estimated to be about 2.1 million yuan, and it can irrigate 982,000 mu of land.

In addition, there are two projects planned to be repaired: the Jingyuan Be灣 River project and the Tianshui Wei River dike project, which are estimated to cost more than 198,000 yuan and can silt up more than 40,000 mu of paddy fields. If the above-mentioned projects are completed, the number of paddy fields will not be less than 3.73 million mu, which is less than 2/10 of the total number of paddy fields. According to the survey in 1928, the population of Gansu Province was about 5.68 million, with an average of only 0.6 mu of paddy fields per person. The amount of grain produced per mu, according to the ordinary situation, is about 400 catties, which is just enough to meet the average person's annual food needs. Now the difference is almost half. Once there is a drought year, it is impossible to avoid famine. Therefore, if you want to consolidate Gansu water conservancy, I think the population should be the center, and first seek to have one mu of paddy field per person, as the minimum limit. Not only should the above-mentioned unfinished projects and the proposed projects be carried out as soon as possible, but also more canals should be added or wells should be dug in the plateau to benefit people's livelihood. If the amount of irrigation can reach more than 2 million mu, then even in a drought year, the people of Gansu Province can be free from worry about food. Not only that, but in the future, when immigrants colonize the border, they can also increase the number of paddy fields according to this standard as the standard for implementation. However, currently, increasing the canals for this irrigation of more than 2 million mu, or the distribution of digging wells, according to the local situation, the ratio of the two projects is 3/4 to 1/4. 3/4 should be 1.5 million mu, and irrigation by canals should be adopted. The cost per mu, according to the average labor price of opening canals in the past, is about 2.2 yuan, so the total amount is about 2.3 million yuan. 1/4 should be 500,000 mu, and digging wells for irrigation should be selected. According to the Shaanxi well digging plan, the types of wells can be divided into free-flowing wells and water-drawing wells. The water output of a free-flowing well can supply 45 mu of paddy fields, and a water-drawing well can supply 40 mu of paddy fields. The labor cost of one well is about 100 yuan (50 yuan for wages and food, 40 yuan for equipment and materials, and 10 yuan for miscellaneous expenses). The traffic in Gansu is blocked, and materials are scarce, so the wages per well should be increased by 20% compared with Shaanxi, and each well should cost about 120 yuan. However, free-flowing wells are not easy to dig. Now, if 500,000 mu are all calculated as配凿water-drawing wells, then 12,500 wells will be dug, and the total cost of the project is about 1.5 million yuan. To sum up, the cost of the various projects of adding, planning to dig, and unfinished projects is about 7.14 million yuan, which can increase more than 3 million mu of paddy fields. Each mu can increase the yield of more than 300 catties of main and miscellaneous grains. More than 3 million mu should increase more than 9 million dan. If each dan is calculated at an average of 4 yuan, the annual profit is about 36 million yuan. In addition to the project cost, there is a surplus profit of more than 28 million yuan. After that, the annual income and the increase in land prices are even more immeasurable. However, the people of Gansu are poor and have difficulty with finances, and are unable to undertake this great cause. The great benefits are endless, and we cannot but hope that all sectors will find ways to invest and develop as much as possible.
