Jiangxi Province Population in Bandit Areas Drops Sharply Yongxin Population Less Than Half 83

Nanchang Correspondence: In the areas occupied by bandits, due to the arbitrary killings by the Red Army, conscription, and extraction of laborers, deaths followed one after another, and production decreased. Therefore, in the newly recovered areas, only a small number of remaining elderly and weak people were left. The rest either died or fled. The population has decreased sharply, and there is a severe shortage of young men. There is land but no one to cultivate it, which is the most serious phenomenon. Although there is no way to count the deaths in each bandit area, according to a letter from Yongxin, the population of the area was originally 300,000. Now that the compilation and investigation of each area has been completed, it is less than half of what it used to be. There are also other counties that are less than 1/3 or 1/4, which can be said to be tragic. (2nd)

Newly Recovered Areas in Southern Jiangxi Six Counties Are Free of Drugs The Military Headquarters Is Designated as an Absolutely Prohibited Opium Area 84

Nanchang Correspondence: The newly recovered bandit areas in southern Jiangxi, such as Ruijin, Huichang, Yudu, Dianguo, Ningdu, and Shicheng, have been occupied by bandits for six or seven years, and have been under strict blockade for nearly five or six years. Various drugs such as opium, heroin, and morphine have not flowed in at all, and have long been forbidden. Opium addicts have also been swept away. Shao Hongji, the Administrative Inspector of the area, believed that since drugs had disappeared in the six counties under his jurisdiction, they should no longer be allowed to re-emerge. He specially asked the military headquarters to approve the designation of the area as an absolutely prohibited opium area, strictly prohibiting the trafficking, smoking, transportation, and planting of opium. The provincial government, the Pacification Headquarters, and the 3rd Route Army have now strictly prohibited it in accordance with this plan. Once discovered, they will be severely punished by military law, so as to ensure that drugs are completely isolated from this area. (2nd)

Songjiang Opium Addict Licenses Reissued on a Regular Basis 85

The implementation of opium prohibition in our province has a four-year prohibition plan. Opium addict licenses were issued in October of last year, and the validity period expired at the end of March. The first batch of opium addicts who should be sent for rehabilitation have also been verified by the Opium Prohibition Committee and notification slips have been drafted and distributed to each district office for distribution at the address, in order to gradually reduce the number of opium addicts. The second phase of license renewal has been prepared by the Prohibition Committee and announced to be from the 11th to the 20th of this month, and will still be reissued at each district office. You must bring two 2-inch photos of yourself. The Class A photo fee is twelve yuan, and the Class B photo fee is one yuan and two jiao. If you do not renew your license after the deadline, you will be punished as a private smoker once you are discovered.

莘莊 Town Residents Present Silver Shield to Inspector Qu 86

Since assuming his post, Inspector Qu Shaoquan of the Sixth Branch of the Xin Zhuang Township Police Station has intensified local defense, resulting in the eradication of theft and false accusations, and the flight of petty criminals. All the residents of the district deeply appreciate his efforts. On the sixth of this month, the entire populace of the town publicly presented him with a silver shield, engraved with the four characters "Lü Yan An Ning" (Peace and Tranquility in the Neighborhoods) to commemorate his service. During the presentation, firecrackers exploded, and the streets were thronged with onlookers.

Nanhui: Robbery Occurs at the West City Gate 87

At the Yuan He Rice Shop outside the West Gate, near the city wall, at about one o'clock last night, suddenly over a dozen thugs speaking with a Hakka accent and with their faces concealed by cloth, arrived armed with box guns and pistols. They first deployed themselves at locations such as the city gate drawbridge, while another five or six broke into the middle gate of the shop. They tied up the shop owner Zheng Kunsheng's wife, Wang, the shop assistant Shi Jisheng, and four others, and then proceeded to rob the place. It is estimated that silver, banknotes, clothing, and other items worth over 500 yuan were stolen. The case was reported by the First District Public Office to the county government. County Magistrate Yuan visited the scene to investigate and set a deadline for solving the case.

Execution of Convicted Thief Gu A'nan 88

The thief Gu A'nan, together with accomplices such as Wang Xiang'an, robbed the property of Xi Ji's family in Yangjiawan, Third District, last December. They also kidnapped Xi's son, Xichun, and demanded a ransom. Subsequently, the Luhui Chamber of Commerce apprehended the criminals Gu A'nan, Wang Xiang'an, and the kidnapped Xichun. After interrogation by the county, Gu A'nan was sentenced to death. This was submitted to the Jiangsu High Court and then to the provincial government for approval by telegraph. At 5 PM yesterday, Gu A'nan was brought to court, his identity was verified, and he was escorted to the execution ground outside the South Gate to be shot.

Suzhou: Villagers in Mudu Township Robbed 89

Genlin, son of Xiang Nong Ru Rushan, a thirty-year-old villager from the fifth Tu of the fourteenth Du in Shen Dian Village, Jinshan Township, Mudu, had planted several mu of vegetable seeds in the open space in front of his door. He had also built a grass shed next to the field and stayed there every night to watch over his crops. At 1:30 AM yesterday (the 6th), suddenly twenty to thirty bandits came from the direction of Lion Mountain, all unarmed. They first went to the Stone family’s house to search. They seemed to be quite familiar with the Stone family's situation. Finding Stone absent, having lodged with a neighbor, they scaled the low wall, opened the door, and searched for a long time. Finding nothing, they tied up Genlin tightly and beat him on the head with a club. Genlin fainted from the pain. When he woke up, the bandits forced him to reveal where the silver was hidden. Genlin told them he had no money. The bandits, thinking that Genlin was deliberately concealing the truth, subjected him to cruel torture, causing him to be burned and to pass out again. The bandits then left. Afterwards, Shi Rushan sent Genlin to Dr. Yan Guansong in Mudu for treatment, but his injuries were severe and his life was in great danger.

Tragic Wall Collapse on Guanqian Street 90

The façade wall of the three-story building of the Suhua Store and Ruihua Shoe Store on Guanqian Street in Suzhou suddenly collapsed at around 6 PM on the afternoon of the 5th. At that time, Guanqian Street was crowded with pedestrians. Three people were injured: Wu Yifeng, a resident of Da Shitou Lane, suffered fractures in his right ulna and ankle; Wu Yifeng's wife, Wu Pang Bingwei, suffered a six-inch laceration on her scalp; and Jing Xiaoliutou, suffered a fracture in his right ulna and a laceration on his head. Several others suffered minor injuries. Wu Yifeng and the other two were sent to the Baoan Hospital for treatment, as their injuries were serious and life-threatening. After the accident, the police district authorities arrested Feng Ruiqing, the owner of Ruihua Store, and Xia Xiusheng, the owner of Suhua Store, and handed them over to the Public Security Bureau for questioning.

Re-Investigation of City and Township Baojia by Groups 91

County Magistrate Wu Qiyun and Liu Jianyuan, the Baojia instructor from the Department of Civil Affairs, found many inaccuracies during the spot checks of the Baojia work in the first district of the city and township. Therefore, yesterday morning (the 6th), they, together with personnel from the Public Security Bureau and the District Public Office, dispatched personnel in four groups to conduct a thorough household re-investigation to rectify the errors.

Wuxi: Seizure of Property to Offset Unpaid Land Tax 92

The arrears of old and new land taxes in this county amount to over one million yuan. Despite repeated strict demands for payment from the provincial authorities and the dispatch of Commissioner Huang Xinlai to urge collection, only over 50,000 yuan has been collected to date. Over 200 grain households have been arrested and pursued for their inability to pay. Commissioner Huang, with the silkworm season approaching, yesterday convened a meeting with tax collection officials. It was decided to make a concerted effort to pursue tax collection before the silkworm season, focusing on large households. At the same time, the heads of various agencies and district and township leaders would be asked to assist. Those grain households who still failed to pay would have their property seized to offset the debt, in order to emphasize the importance of national taxation. Commissioner Huang also strictly forbade tax collection officials from extortion and blackmail.

Drastic Weather Changes Affect Sericulture 93

The weather this spring has been drastically fluctuating. After a period of warm weather last month, it was followed by severe cold and snowfall. This has severely impacted the sprouting mulberry leaves, causing significant damage. Moreover, the total number of spring silkworm eggs in Jiangsu Province this year is over 900,000, raising concerns about a shortage of mulberry leaves for the spring silkworms. Currently, various sericulture farms in Jiangsu Province are actively transporting spring cocoons to Zhejiang Province for sale, and over 200,000 have already been exported. However, to prevent a shortage of eggs within the province, the provincial government has sent officials to Hushu Pass to dissuade merchants from continuing to export to Zhejiang. Upon hearing this news, various sericulture farms in this county believe that if they are not allowed to export, there will be an oversupply in the future. Therefore, they will convene a meeting of fellow sericulturists in the coming days to discuss the pros and cons and seek a solution.

Elderly Couple Suddenly Announce Divorce 94

Sun Zhibei, a resident of Xin Xianqian in the city, is 75 years old and has been married to the boat woman Qiao Xian for over 30 years. Qiao Xian is now 55 years old, and they have no children. In his middle age, Sun opened the Qingyuan Teahouse in Beimen Tantou Lane, which gained a good reputation. He also accumulated some savings. In recent years, Sun's circumstances have declined sharply, and his environment has deteriorated. However, the old couple's relationship was still quite good. However, recently, for some unknown reason, the elderly couple suddenly announced their divorce. The agreement has already been signed, with Qiao Xian paying Sun 850 yuan to cover his retirement and funeral expenses.

Changzhou: County Government Discusses the Problem of Raft Parking on the Canal 95

The various trade associations of towns such as Wuyi Weicun and Wangxiacun submitted a petition to the Department of Construction, stating that parking log rafts on the canal obstructs traffic and is prone to causing silting. They requested that raft parking on the canal be prohibited after the completion of the current canal dredging project. The Department of Construction ordered the county government to investigate and handle the matter. County Magistrate Hou considered that the timber industry is a major industry in the county, so he convened a meeting with representatives of the industry at the county government on the afternoon of the 5th. Xu Juxi, Qi Zhenyuan, and others attended and submitted a petition, stating the obligations that the industry had fulfilled for the canal and the reasons that it did not obstruct silting. County Magistrate Hou proposed that regulations be formulated to ensure that raft parking does not obstruct traffic. The representatives agreed to discuss and draft regulations with merchants when they arrived in Changzhou and then submit them for review. The meeting was then adjourned. The County Magistrate plans to submit the timber industry's petition to the next administrative meeting for discussion and then forward it to the Department of Construction for review.

Zhenjiang: Provincial Government Plans to Build a Radio Station 96

The provincial government plans to build a radio station to promote party principles, disseminate government policies, and assist in projects such as guiding the Huai River and banning opium. The Secretariat is responsible for the planning, and the site has been selected on the square next to the Department of Civil Affairs. Poles are currently being erected, and broadcasting is expected to begin soon. The new meteorological observatory built by the Department of Construction, located on the summit of Beigu Mountain, was completed last month and has been open to the public for several days. It has been attracting large crowds of visitors.

Yangzhou: Business Tax Dispute Becomes Serious Again 97

Previously, the Business Tax Bureau of this county, based on the instructions of the Provincial Committee, sent personnel to inspect the account books of various shops. They detained and sent to the county government for punishment the shop assistants of the Zhenda Candle and Charcoal Shop and the Baofeng Yikang Cloth Shop in Duozijie, who refused to submit their account books for inspection. Initially, the merchants were indignant. However, after Chairman Teng of the Chamber of Commerce mediated and repeatedly petitioned the Provincial Committee member Yan, who came to Yangzhou to supervise the inspection, the Provincial Committee proposed three key points, which most merchants accepted. Unexpectedly, yesterday (the 5th), the conditions on both sides changed again. The shop assistants detained by the county government have not yet been released on bail. As a result, today, all cloth shops, candle and charcoal shops, and incense shops have gone on strike, posting signs on their doors that read "The Business Tax Bureau uses violence and coercion, arresting shop employees, public anger leads to suspension of business." In addition, they published "A Declaration of Suspension of Business by Merchants Due to the Abuse of Power, Violence, and Arrest of Merchants by Investigators of the Business Tax Bureau." As a result, the case has become serious again. Provincial Committee member Yan Shudong came to Yangzhou from Zhen in the afternoon to resolve the situation. Currently, representatives of various industries are gathered at a meeting of the Chamber of Commerce. It is said that the leaders of the various businesses are advocating a peaceful approach, and Provincial Committee member Yan is also not in favor of excessive demands.

Nantong: Teams from Six Counties Gather in Nantong 98

The Civil Group Security Teams of six counties, Nantong, Rugao, Haimen, Qidong, Jingjiang, and Chongming, as well as the Industrial Security Teams of Tongtai Haiqi, have been ordered by the Fourth District Security Headquarters to gather in Nantong to await inspection by the Director of the Security Department, Xiang Zhizhao.

Jiangyin: Financial and Construction Departments Approve Loan for Dredging Huangtiangang by Telegraph 100

County Magistrate Yan stated that the local area needed to raise 95,000 yuan to dredge the Huangtiangang Southern Canal. He originally intended to levy a ship tax to offset the loan, but the provincial departments refused to allow the tax, as it was considered burdensome. The county government then established a Huangtiangang Dredging Committee, which decided to use the retained county road construction mu tax and 70% of the water conservancy fees as collateral to negotiate sales with various banks in Wuxi. Yesterday (the 4th), the Financial and Construction Departments telegraphed back their approval to proceed accordingly.

Robbery and Murder in Houmei Town 101

The family of Xu Hesheng, a farmer from Xiaomeijia Village, Cangshan Township, Houmei Town, Seventh District, had a daughter getting married the other day and had quite a dowry, which was coveted by thieves. They plotted to steal it but failed. On the night of the 3rd, suddenly seven or eight bandits, armed with box guns and flashlights, went to Xu's house to rob. Xu Hesheng escaped and cried for help, alarming his neighbor Mei Fusheng, who suspected that they were thieves. He chased after them with a door bar, but was shot by the bandits, hitting him in the throat. He fell to the ground and died. Xu's family suffered heavy losses. On the 5th, the district office reported the matter to the county, and Zhou Cheng, the county magistrate, sent officials to the village to conduct an examination.

Hefei: County Territory Re-divided into Six District Offices 102

The territory of Hefei County is the largest in the province, with a population of 1.3 million. The original nine districts were revised and agreed to be six district offices in recent days at meetings of various public groups and gentry at the county government. (1) The area within thirty li of the city and the county seat is designated as the First District, with the district office located in the county seat. (2) East One, East Two, East Er Township, Northeast Two and Four Districts are designated as the Second District, with the district office located at Xishan Post. (3) South Five, South Six, South Seven Three Districts, and Southwest One, Southwest Three, east of Anhe Road, south of Shuliu Road, are designated as the Third District, with the district office located in Sanhe Town. (4) West One, West Two, Southwest Two and Three Districts, and Southwest One, Southwest Two, west of Anhe Road, north of Shuliu Road, are designated as the Fourth District, with the district office located in Guanting Town. (5) North One, North Two, Northwest Town Three Districts are designated as the Fifth District, with the district office located in Shuangdunji. (6) Northeast One, Northeast Three, Four, and Five Districts are designated as the Sixth District, with the district office located in Wangzicheng. The county government has now submitted the plan to the provincial government for implementation.

President Sun Talks About Dividing Central and Local Authority. The Legislative Yuan Studies the Issue Separately According to Central Regulations. Supports Chairman Chiang's National Economic Construction. 103

According to the Central News Agency, Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, together with Yu Youren, President of the Control Yuan, and Dai Jitao, President of the Examination Yuan, left Nanjing by night train the night before last at 11:00 PM and arrived at the North Station in Shanghai at 7:20 AM yesterday. They immediately returned to their private residences to rest. President Sun received reporters from various newspapers at his private residence on Columbia Road at around 11:00 AM. He stated that, regarding the issue of dividing central and local authority, the Central Political Council had formulated principles based on six guidelines and submitted them to the National Government, which in turn ordered the Legislative Yuan to formulate regulations separately within the scope of their respective responsibilities. The Legislative Yuan has now assigned them to the relevant committees for separate study according to the principles set by the Central Government. Chairman Chiang's proposal for the National Economic Construction Movement is very meaningful. In my opinion, the government must first raise funds to implement basic projects to promote national economic construction. As for abolishing excessive taxes, this has now been completely achieved. The provision in the Stock Exchange Law to prohibit government officials from engaging in speculative trading is for the benefit of the stock exchange, to prevent the spread of rumors and disruption of the market. I hope that all government officials will be able to perform their duties and abide by the law, and abandon the business of engaging in speculative trading. Chiang Tso-ping, our ambassador to Japan, visited Taiwan this time for inspection purposes and had no other mission.

South Seas Tycoon Suggests Saving South Seas Commerce By Establishing a National Goods Introduction Center to Facilitate Sales. 106

According to the Shen Shi News Agency, Chen Xixian, manager of the South Seas Chinese Trade Company, returned to China from Java and met with He Bingxian, director of the International Trade Bureau, to discuss the development of trade with the Dutch East Indies. Chen also provided a written opinion, which is excerpted as follows:

The Foundation of Overseas Chinese Economy Is Shaken. The economic situation in the Dutch East Indies has been affected by the global economic downturn in recent years, causing panic. However, due to its political stability and sound fiscal adjustments, it is still a market for international trade. Therefore, Japan is making every effort to operate there. In addition to the Kobe-Java and Taiwan-Java routes, it has also opened a new Hong Kong-Java route. This will inevitably lead to maritime competition with the shipping companies operated by the Dutch, and competition has recently broken out. Although this is unlikely to cause any political changes, free confrontation between merchants of both sides will begin, which will negatively affect commerce. The foundation of the overseas Chinese economy is also being shaken as a result.

The Dutch and Japanese Are Organizing Associations. Due to the above reasons, both the Dutch and Japanese sides are organizing associations to cope with the situation. There is the Japanese Commercial Porcelain Association, and the Dutch East Indies has the Dutch East Indies Commercial Association. Overseas Chinese also have the All Dutch East Indies Chinese Commercial Association. The Chinese Commercial Association was organized in October last year and has been in existence for half a year, but it has not yet achieved any special effectiveness. In addition, there are a small number of national goods companies, which are also difficult to compete with the Japanese and Dutch due to the lack of overseas commercial assistance agencies.

A Commercial Plan to Aid Overseas Chinese. Therefore, in order to aid the economy of overseas Chinese, a Chinese goods introduction center should be established in commercial areas that are thriving and suitable in the South Seas. (1) The purpose is to connect overseas Chinese merchants and domestic factories, establish a direct relationship, and enable the government's foreign economic plans to be implemented. (2) The mission is to contact domestic factories and promote sales on their behalf, and to purchase national goods on behalf of overseas Chinese merchants. (3) The work includes propaganda, introduction, investigation, research, design, national goods exhibitions, and commercial intelligence reports. (4) The organization will be sponsored by the National Trade Bureau, with the assistance of the Shanghai and Java consuls to carry out the work. In this way, our economy in the Dutch East Indies will be revitalized.

British Silver Reportedly Being Shipped to Shanghai Today and Tomorrow. 107

Reporters from the Shiye News Agency learned from the business departments and foreign exchange departments of the Central, China, and Communications Banks that the second batch of silver shipped by the Great Britain Company's Lazquhao ship, totaling 2,925,000 yuan, is scheduled to enter the port at 7:00 AM this morning (the 7th) and dock at the Gonghexiang Wharf in Hongkou. It is expected that the China, Communications, and Third Banks will send personnel to be responsible for unloading tomorrow. At that time, the China, Communications, and Third Banks will also send personnel to deposit it in the vaults of the Bank of China, in the same location as the second batch. Transfer of Properties in Shanghai of the Chinese Eastern Railway Still Not Completed. No New Developments in the Legal Aspect. 108

According to the Central News Agency, the Japanese United News Agency reported that the various properties of the Chinese Eastern Railway in this city have been taken over. However, the Central News Agency reporters learned from various sources that the South Manchurian Railway Office stated that it has not yet taken over the properties. The former Sino-Russian Daosheng Bank has filed an appeal regarding the rights relationship and sought to recover the outstanding debt. Yang Ruinian, the lawyer representing the case, told reporters that the report that the case was not accepted was incorrect. This is not a criminal lawsuit, and there is no such provision. The court should hold a hearing. However, the legal procedures are time-consuming, so there are no developments at present. It is also understood that the South Manchurian Railway Office is currently reviewing the properties and will not take them over if there is no substantial benefit. The number of properties of the Chinese Eastern Railway in Shanghai is not large.

Guo Chuntao Returns from Inspection in Europe. Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon. Will Return to Nanjing to Report After a Short Rest. 109

Former official Guo Chuntao was dispatched to Europe and the United States last spring to inspect industries. More than a year has passed. He has visited more than ten countries, including England, France, Belgium, Germany, Hungary, Austria, Switzerland, and Italy. He has now completed his mission and returned to China on the Conte Verde. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon. The ship docked at the Pudong Wharf at around 4:00 PM. Guo's family and dozens of relatives and friends gathered at the New Customs Wharf at 2:00 PM and took a company launch to greet him. After Guo shook hands with the welcoming party, reporters immediately asked him about the main tasks and feelings of this trip on the launch. He replied as follows: I (Guo himself) was dispatched abroad last year to inspect general industries in Europe. However, due to time constraints, I paid more attention to agriculture and industry. As far as the countries I visited are concerned, in 1934, whether it was production, trade, unemployment, etc., in general, on the surface, there was a trend of improvement. However, in its origin, either due to currency inflation, or due to the development of military industry, and other artificial methods, this is only a temporary stimulus, and it may be difficult to get rid of the crisis of panic. The deepest impression we gained from visiting various European countries is "preparedness for war" and "unemployment." Observing the current situation, it is feared that the Second World War may still break out in Europe. If so, the international position of our country will be even more difficult. Because of the fatigue of the journey, Guo finished speaking and took the launch across the river. It is heard that Guo is temporarily staying at the New Asia Hotel on North Sichuan Road. He will stay in Shanghai for a day or two to visit relatives and friends and take a short rest before going to Nanjing to report.

Arts Exhibition Preview Opens Tomorrow: President Wang and Others to Visit; Minister Wang Inspects Venue, Highly Satisfied 110

Central News Agency: The Shanghai preview exhibition organized by the Preparatory Committee for the International Exhibition of Chinese Art in London is now ready and scheduled to open tomorrow (the 8th). Government officials will be invited for inspection this morning (the 7th), and Shanghai gentry, foreign guests, and related parties will be invited this afternoon. President Wang of the Executive Yuan and key figures from the Party and government are expected to attend. British Ambassador Sir Miles Lampson and many consular officials will also be present. This preview features a systematic exhibition of ancient and modern Chinese artworks, a pioneering effort in China. Domestic archaeologists, artists, and people from all walks of life are expected to take great interest. A Central News Agency reporter visited the person in charge and toured the venue in detail, and will provide a systematic report to the nation.

Background of the Initiative: The exhibition was originally proposed last year by the British Universities China Committee and British academics, following the precedent of international art exhibitions held in London by Italy, France, the Netherlands, Belgium, and Iran. They consulted with our ambassador to the UK, Mr. Guo, and sought our consent. The government, recognizing the unique value and status of Chinese art in world cultural history, believed that an international exhibition could deepen Western understanding of Chinese culture and expressed willingness to consider it. After multiple discussions, it was decided to hold the exhibition at the Royal Academy in London's Burlington House, under the joint supervision of the Chinese and British governments and managed by a council composed of Chinese and British individuals. The exhibition is scheduled to run from November this year to March next year, lasting approximately sixteen weeks.

Organization of the Preparatory Committee: Considering the matter important, the Executive Yuan established a preparatory committee in China to oversee the exhibition, which was formed in October last year.

Initiation of the Preview Exhibition: To allow domestic audiences to preview the valuable exhibits, the preparatory committee decided at its second meeting to hold a preview exhibition in Shanghai before the exhibits were sent abroad and another exhibition in Nanjing upon their return, providing Chinese people with the opportunity to see, hear about, study, and reference the artworks. Once the decision was made, it was submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. Simultaneously, the former site of the Bank of China on the Shanghai Bund was rented to serve as the office, marking the origin of the preview exhibition.

Months of Preparation: The committee's tasks were quite complex, especially the selection, preservation, transportation, and security of the exhibits. Therefore, the committee established specialized committees for exhibit selection, preservation, and preview exhibition preparation. With the collaborative efforts of various personnel, the preparations were completed in just two to three months.

Categories and Sources: The exhibits collected by the committee are divided into five major categories: 1. Bronzes, 2. Ceramics, 3. Calligraphy and Painting, 4. Miscellaneous Items (including Jade, Carved Lacquer, Cloisonné Enamel, Embroidery, Folding Fans, Ancient Books, Oracle Bones and Stone Tools), and 5. Antiquities from the Academia Sinica. The sources include the National Palace Museum, the Antiquities Exhibition Office of the Ministry of Interior, the Academia Sinica, the National Library of Peiping, Yenching University and Peking University, the Henan Museum, and the provincial libraries of Shandong and Anhui. The majority of the exhibits are selected from the National Palace Museum and the Antiquities Exhibition Office. In terms of age, the selected items represent various periods from ancient times to the recent past, each systematically arranged according to its historical development. The standards are extremely strict, with Chinese and five British experts meticulously researching and carefully selecting the items. Items with special characteristics are carefully retained by the preparatory committee to avoid sending them abroad. The selected items are cataloged, photographed, and published for research and reference.

Comprehensive Security Measures: The committee has implemented comprehensive security measures for the exhibits. During the exhibition in Shanghai, the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Shanghai Municipal Council have provided significant support in terms of protection, fire prevention, and security, including iron fences, iron nets, alarms, and other equipment, as witnessed by reporters. For overseas transportation, round-trip transport will be provided by British warships, with Chinese personnel accompanying the exhibits.

Various Aspects of the Exhibition: The exhibition is scheduled to run from April 8th to April 30th, with closures on Saturday mornings, except for the opening day. Admission tickets are priced at two yuan each. To save costs, most of the staff members are seconded from the National Palace Museum, the Antiquities Exhibition Office, and the Ministry of Education.

Unprecedented Effort: Ancient Chinese art has been on display at the National Palace Museum in Peiping and the Antiquities Exhibition Office for many years, attracting numerous visitors. However, previous exhibitions were scattered and disorganized, with a mix of fine and ordinary items, making research difficult for archaeologists and artists. Now, experts have carefully selected, organized, and arranged exhibits such as bronzes, ceramics, and calligraphy and painting, systematically presenting them from ancient times to the modern era according to their development sequence. This allows viewers to understand the origins and development of various art forms, which is unprecedented. Shanghai offers a variety of entertainment venues, but none can compare to this exhibition. Some of the exhibits, such as ancient bronzes, famous porcelains, and calligraphy and paintings, have rarely been seen in a lifetime. Due to the original storage of National Palace Museum artifacts in Shanghai, Shanghai residents are fortunate to be among the first to view them, a rare opportunity that makes them more fortunate than people living in any other era or location. It is hoped that this exhibition will cultivate an appreciation for high-quality entertainment and promote a passion for art among Shanghai residents.

Minister Wang Inspects: Minister of Education Wang Shijie, a member of the preparatory committee, arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and visited the venue at 2 PM that afternoon, expressing his satisfaction. After hosting a banquet for the preservation committee members and the British Consul yesterday, he revisited the venue for inspection.

Reception Without Ceremony: This morning, 127 invitations were sent to members of the National Government and the Central Party Headquarters. This afternoon, approximately 200 people, including foreign envoys, consular officials, Chinese diplomats, and journalists, will be invited. The reception will not involve any formal ceremony, and the same applies to the public opening tomorrow.

Unexhibited Artifacts: Some of the artifacts being shipped to London for the exhibition have never been displayed, including furniture and stationery used by the Qing Emperor Qianlong. The committee decided not to display these items due to their limited significance.

Rules for Visiting: 1. Visiting hours are from 9:00 AM to 4:30 PM. 2. Visitors must present a ticket for admission, valid for one person on the day of issue only. Expired tickets are invalid. 3. Individuals with infectious diseases or under the age of ten are not allowed to enter. 4. Visitors are not allowed to bring items or equipment into the venue. Umbrellas, walking sticks, and cameras must be deposited at the cloakroom. 5. Visitors must present their admission ticket to the ticket inspector at the entrance for verification and corner clipping. 6. Smoking and eating are strictly prohibited inside the venue. 7. Copying, photographing, and making noise are strictly prohibited inside the venue. 8. Re-entry requires purchasing another ticket. 9. Visitors should proceed in an orderly manner and refrain from wandering back and forth. 10. Visitors must not touch any exhibits and should be careful not to bump into display cases or tear off seals. Visitors will be held liable for any damage to exhibits. 11. Visitors must return their admission ticket to the ticket collector upon exiting. 12. Venue staff members will correct any violations of the above rules.

Preface to the Antiquities Catalog: The following is the original text of the preface to the catalog of antiquities for the International Exhibition of Chinese Art in London, Republic of China, October 23rd year. The National Government of the Republic of China has decided to select and send national artworks to London for international exhibition, with the aim of allowing Westerners to see the greatness and beauty of Chinese art. A preparatory committee was organized to handle the matter. The preparatory committee believes that the most important task is the selection of exhibits. Therefore, several art experts were selected and formed a specialized committee to be responsible for the selection. The specialized committee was established in November of this year and has been collecting and studying for several months. In the meantime, opinions were exchanged with British experts, and the selection was finalized. This catalog is specially edited to serve as a reference and for verification and research. This is how the catalog was made. According to the catalog, the types of exhibits are ploughs, ceramics, calligraphy and painting, jade, carved red, cloisonne, embroidery, folding fans, ancient books, etc. The development of Chinese art, from ancient times to the present, is briefly outlined. The exhibiting institutions are the Palace Museum, the Ancient Artifacts Exhibition Hall, the Academia Sinica, the Peiping Library, the Henan Museum, and the Anhui Provincial Library. The most selected items are from the Palace Museum and the Ancient Artifacts Exhibition Hall. This is a general overview. April 24th year of the Republic of China, Preparatory Committee for the International Exhibition of Chinese Art in London.

Statistics of Antiquities: According to the general catalog, the antiquities for this exhibition are statistically as follows: Bronzes account for 23 pages, ceramics 59 pages, calligraphy and painting 36 pages, and others (including embroidery, jade, cloisonné, carved red, folding fans, rare ancient books) 30 pages. (Bronzes) 1. Origin of Chinese bronzes, 2. Types of bronzes, 3. Era of bronzes, 4. Region of bronzes, 5. Artistic value of Chinese bronzes, 6. Historical value of Chinese bronzes, 7. Overview of this exhibition. Zheng bronze group, 8 pieces, B. Shouxian bronze group, 4 pieces, totaling 108 pieces. (Ceramics) General introduction by expert Guo Baochang (1) Origin of ceramics, (2) Famous kilns of past dynasties, (3) Ceramic body, (4) Ceramic glaze, (5) Ceramic patterns, (6) Jingdezhen kiln, (7) Enamel color porcelain. The exhibits include 8 Song kilns, 7 Southern Song kilns, 2 Jin kilns, 3 Yuan kilns, 12 Ming kilns, and 17 Qing kilns, totaling 346 pieces. (Calligraphy and Painting) (1) Tang Dynasty calligraphy and painting 3, (2) Five Dynasties calligraphy and painting 2, (3) Song Dynasty calligraphy and painting 55, (4) Yuan Dynasty calligraphy and painting 41, (5) Ming Dynasty calligraphy and painting 43, (6) Qing Dynasty calligraphy and painting 29, totaling 173 pieces. (Others) (1) Embroidery 29 pieces, (2) Jade 70 pieces, (3) Cloisonné 16 pieces, (4) Carved red 5 pieces, (5) Folding fans 20 pieces, (6) Rare ancient books 30 pieces, (still have 20 kinds not yet arrived) totaling 170 pieces.

Contents of Antiquities: As for the contents of the antiquities, bronzes are divided into Li, Yan, Ding, Dun, Fu, Gui, Xu, Dou, Hu, Zun, Pan, and Zhong. For example, Father Xin Li, Woman Ding, Chen Hou Wu Dun, Shao Shushan Father Fu, Taotie pattern Gui, Shuo Ji Xian Xu, and Xingqiu Dou. Chenghua kiln, glaze to be bright red three fish, large bowl, Qing Kangxi kiln, bright red radish Zun, Qing Kangxi seal kiln, ruby Guanyin bottle, etc. Calligraphy and painting include Tang Dynasty Li A Glimpse of the Venue: Yesterday afternoon, a Central News Agency reporter specially visited the exhibition. At the entrance of the old site of the Bank of China, a plaque of "London International Exhibition of Chinese Art Shanghai Preview Exhibition" with yellow background and green characters has been hung. On the platform are several pots of verdant potted plants. Entering is a large lounge. Books such as Palace Museum picture albums are distributed throughout the room and are being displayed to be sold at the public exhibition. The chairs in the room are all made of chrome. There are no decorations on the walls, but there are various kinds of trees standing tall and low, sparse and dense. When asked, I learned that it was displayed by artist Situ Qiao. Behind the room, follow the arrow of the road sign and enter the exhibition hall. The displays here are mostly ancient paintings and embroideries, which are hung on specially made double walls by copper pulleys. In order to avoid the weight of the lower end of the painting shaft being difficult to bear, cloth straps are used to hang them up. It can be seen that the experts have put a lot of thought into the display. In addition to ancient paintings on the second floor, there are nearly a hundred steel-framed glass cabinets, in which bronzes, jade, folding fans, cloisonné, porcelain, ancient books, carved red (lacquerware) and the "Archaeological Selection Example" item from the Academia Sinica that arrived the latest are displayed a hundred pieces of ancient objects, such as tortoise shells used for divination during the stock era, and stone tools from ancient times, etc. Each ancient object has a card with categories, names, writers, times, owners, and notes, which are filled in Chinese and English, so that the audience can understand it at a glance. The process of a certain ancient object, and the conference printed a Chinese and English detailed catalog each, the description is detailed, quite enough to be the blue book when appreciating ancient objects.

Wang Cai Visited Yesterday: When the Central News Agency reporter visited the exhibition yesterday, Education Minister Wang Shijie, Academia Sinica President Cai Yuanpei, and four British committee members were also visiting the exhibition and browsed various ancient items for a long time, and the five British committee members praised them very much.

In Progress Shanghai-Guangdong Wireless Telephone to be Operational Before Double Tenth Festival 111

Central News Agency reports that the Ministry of Communications, recognizing the increasingly close relationship between Shanghai and Guangdong, instructed the International Telecommunications Bureau to prepare for long-distance telephone service between Shanghai and Guangdong. First Three Months of This Year Shanghai Cargo to US Statistics No Silver Shipped to US 112

The US Consul General in Shanghai yesterday released statistics on Shanghai's exports to the US for the first three months of this year. Various goods were worth a total of US$5,521,554. A check revealed that the same period last year was US$3,718,906, an increase of more than US$1.8 million. There was no silver shipped from Shanghai to the US in these three months, while silver bars and silver dollars shipped to the US at the same time last year totaled 762,500 ounces, worth more than US$350,000. In the first three months of this year, Shanghai's exports to the US were dominated by inedible plant products (excluding fiber wood), totaling US$1,994,066. The same period last year was only US$81,946, so the increase was huge. The second largest was inedible animal and animal products, totaling US$1,914,033, a significant decrease compared to US$2,374,069 at the same time last year. The third largest was textiles, totaling US$1,241,483, a decrease of slightly more than US$100,000 compared to the same period last year. In addition, Shanghai's exports to the Philippines in the first three months of this year totaled US$254,953, while the same period last year was US$351,371. Exports to Hawaii were US$10,752, while the same period last year was US$11,905.

Strict Crackdown on Bands and Funeral Cars by the Municipal Government Hoping that the public will no longer hire absurd bands and radio hearses 113

The music bands in this city not only have bizarre costumes, but also the music they play is often inappropriate. Sometimes they play sad music or foreign national anthems at festive banquets, or popular songs and ditties at funerals. It is absurd and ridiculous, causing laughter at home and abroad. The Shanghai Municipal Government has ordered the relevant departments to strictly crack down on them. Although a few professionals have followed the instructions to improve, those who do not know how to study are still often found. Recently, there have been hearses equipped with radios, arbitrarily playing songs along the way, which is even more inappropriate. In addition to the Municipal Government again ordering the competent authorities to crack down on them, it is hoped that the public will understand the general situation and no longer hire such bands and cars, so as to show solemnity and promote morality.

Shouchang Ship Employees of Sanbei Shipping Company Positions are Taken in Yichang Major Conflict Occurred 114

The new Shouchang ship of Sanbei Company runs on the Shanghai-Yichang route. Unexpectedly, a major conflict occurred over the seizing of sailors' jobs on the first trip to Yichang. A telegram has been sent to Shanghai stating that the ship will not carry passengers and will return to Shanghai. It has been decided to resolve the conflict in Shanghai. The details are as follows:

Seizing of Jobs: The Shouchang ship, with a deadweight of 630 tons, was fully loaded with cargo from Shanghai to the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, and many passengers took it to Yichang. The stewards and tallymen in the middle cabin department of the ship were all hired in Shanghai before departure. On the 5th of this month, when the ship arrived in Yichang, the local Seafarers' Association led a large number of workers to the dock as soon as the ship arrived. As soon as the passengers disembarked, they forcibly seized and moved all the luggage from the original stewards, and did not allow the staff sent by Shanghai to work on the ship, forcing the middle cabin department to hand over their positions. The crew refused, leading to a major conflict.

Failed Mediation: The Yichang Seafarers' Union forcibly sent workers to the Shouchang ship, including 12 middle cabin stewards and 6 tallymen, regardless of the circumstances, and occupied the cabins without authorization. The staff refused to hand over their positions, so a large number of local workers were invited to the ship, completely expelling the stewards and tallymen sent by Shanghai and ordering them to leave the ship immediately. The Yichang Sanbei Company reported to the local Party, military, and political authorities for mediation, but the Yichang Seafarers' Association firmly refused to budge, resulting in no resolution.

Telegram to Shanghai for Instructions: Yesterday, Sanbei Company received a telegram from Yichang, stating that the Yichang Seafarers' Association forcibly sent workers, 12 in the middle cabin and 6 tallymen, completely expelling the stewards from Shanghai, forcibly taking over passenger luggage, the Yichang security authorities were unable to mediate, fearing that a conflict would occur between the two sides en route, it is proposed not to load passengers, and solve the problem in Shanghai. Now the workers sent by Yichang have boarded the ship and do not allow the Shanghai workers to work. Shouchang has given up passenger service. Yesterday, it has already left Yichang and is returning to Shanghai. The Shanghai head office has decided to convene workers from both sides and conduct a resolution after Shouchang arrives in Shanghai within the next week.

City Land Bureau Issues Notice to Citizens Urging Exchange of Land Certificates 116

The City Land Bureau, in order to facilitate the exchange of certificates and make it easier for the public to understand, has specially prepared a notice to citizens and printed a separate booklet for public reference. The text is as follows:

Notice to Citizens Regarding the Land Bureau's Handling of Certificate Exchange (April 1, 1935). To the citizens of this city who hold land certificates but have not yet exchanged them for land ownership certificates: Since its establishment in the 16th year of the Republic, this Land Bureau has felt that there are too many types of land certificates within the city limits. Furthermore, due to the changes of the times and the relationship between transfer and separation, everything recorded on the certificates is completely inconsistent with the actual situation. People holding such certificates will inevitably feel difficulties everywhere. Therefore, this Bureau decided to handle the exchange of certificates after land survey. The purpose is nothing more than to protect the property rights of the people, so that each household's base can have accurate boundaries. Now, it has been seven or eight years. Over the years, more than ninety parcels of land ownership certificates have been announced for development. According to the Bureau's regulations, owners should, within one month after the announcement of the development, submit the old certificates, grain receipts for the past three years, and other title deeds to the Bureau, and fill out a receipt for the exchange of old certificates, in order to receive the topographical map of the household land later. After receiving the map, if it is deemed to be consistent with the actual situation, sign the map and return it to the Bureau. After three months, you can come to pick up the land certificate.

On the people's side, although many people come to the Bureau to apply within the time limit, there are still quite a few who wait and see. For example, in various areas of the South Shanghai District, the land certificates were developed in the 18th year, and even today, many household lands have not been exchanged. For these lands that have not been exchanged for a long time, the Bureau has decided to take them all back under municipal management, set up public land boundary stones, and all income from the land will also be collected by the government. It will not be returned until the owner of the land obtains a land certificate. Because if this is not done, the land certificates in this city will never be unified. Therefore, this Bureau sincerely hopes that all citizens will actively exchange their land certificates.

The reason why some citizens do not come to exchange certificates may be because: (1) the certificate does not match the grain, (2) the certificate does not match the land, (3) the certificate shows less land than there actually is, (4) the certificate belongs to co-owners, (5) the certificate is mortgaged. As for other reasons, it cannot be said that there are none, but most of them and more important ones are none other than the above. In order to take care of the citizens, this Bureau has stipulated corresponding measures for these shortcomings. Citizens are making a big mistake if they do not come to exchange certificates because of these reasons. Now, let's explain these measures:

(1) If the certificate does not match the grain or the land, naturally the certificate cannot be exchanged. However, as long as the Bureau verifies that the land does belong to the citizen, then after obtaining a guarantee from the four neighbors and paying all grain receipts for the past three years, the certificate can be approved.

(2) If the certificate shows less land than there actually is, the extra land is called overflow land. The Bureau has also set standards for handling overflow land. In August of the 23rd year, it was revised again and several methods were set up for citizens to choose from. That is to say, raising the tax rate is only calculated at 60% of the estimated value. The estimated value is originally lower than the market price, and now it is discounted by 60%. May I ask, citizens, shouldn't these obligations still be fulfilled? (After the owners obtain the maps, if they see that there is overflow land that needs to be taxed, they can inquire about the exact amount of the tax increase from the Second Section at any time for proper preparation).

(3) If a certificate is co-owned by several people, they often push each other and are unwilling to contribute, or even fight and snatch, harboring malicious intentions. Therefore, it is repeatedly delayed. In fact, the co-owners may as well send the co-ownership evidence to the Bureau together for verification and report the co-ownership situation. The Bureau can naturally manage it on behalf of them. If you want to divide the land, it is also very easy. The cost is only some measurement fee and certificate fee.

(4) If the certificate is mortgaged, it cannot be redeemed for a while and cannot be exchanged. The mortgagee, because the certificate is someone else's, is inconvenient to overstep. So they connect with each other and there is no way. In this case, both the mortgagor and the mortgagee can come to the Bureau together to exchange. First, make a land design in the name of the mortgagor, and then write clearly on the certificate who is the mortgagee according to the mortgage registration method. This way, both parties are very stable and do not have to be afraid of either party using any fraudulent means.

In areas where land certificates have not been announced for development, the exchange can of course be postponed. However, if things like mortgages, divisions, or sales occur, you should first come to the Bureau to request measurement and exchange of certificates, because the Bureau does not register mortgages of old certificates. Both the mortgagor and the mortgagee will lose a protection. As for division or sale, there must be accurate acreage, and it is especially necessary to go through the Bureau's measurement and division first. The procedures for this type of request for measurement and exchange of certificates are also very simple. There is no need to submit a formal document, just check all the certificates and send them to the Fourth Section of the Bureau and fill out a receipt for the recovery of the old certificate (if you are anxious to sell it, he can use this receipt to make a contract first), and then, with the receipt, pay the measurement fee and the land protection fee to the Third Section, and a date can be set for measurement. After the measurement, a draft map of the request for measurement will be drawn, and the owner will be notified to come and see it. After the owner signs and returns it, a land certificate can be issued in three months. If there is overflow land, public harbors, and road land included in the tax increase, you only need to pay the tax increase fee and you can get the land certificate in three months.

Now, the parcels of land certificates that have been announced for development are listed below by region. I hope that citizens who have land in these areas will quickly follow the procedures and come to the Bureau to exchange their land certificates. Don't delay any longer and blame yourselves for not acting in time. (Listed below) 24 Bao Fang 11 Tu, 25 Bao 2 Tu, 4 Tu, 5 Tu, 6 Tu, 7 Tu, 8 Tu, 9 Tu, 10 Tu, 11 Tu, 11 Tu, 12 Tu, 14 Tu, 15 Tu, 16 Tu, 27 Bao 1 Tu, 2 Tu, 4 Tu, Jie 1 Tu, Jie 91 Tu, Jie 4 Tu, Que 3 Tu, 27 Bao 10 Tu, 11 Tu, South 12 Tu, North 12 Tu, 8 Tu, 13 Tu, North 12 Tu, 28 Bao 5 Tu, 6 Tu, East 7 Tu, 89 Tu, North 12 Tu, South 12 Tu, 3 Tu, 4 Tu, West 7 Tu, 10 and 11 Tu, South 12 Tu (Tingwei), West 18 Tu, 29 Bao 1 Tu, East 2 Tu, 3 Tu, 4 Tu, 5 Tu, East and West 6 Tu. (Each map in the Pusong District is exchanged at 699 West Fahua Town, which is the old site of the former Township Office, except for South 12 Tu) 24 Bao Small 9 Tu, 26 Bao 10 and 13 Tu, East 11 and West 11 Tu, East 27 and West 27 Tu, 14 Tu, 15 Tu, 22 Tu, East 23 and West 23 Tu, 24 Tu, 25 Tu, 26 Tu, 28 Bao East 16 Tu, East 18 Tu, 22 Bao 51 Tu, 23 Bao 2 Tu, 35 Tu, 47 Tu, 6 Tu, 7 Tu, 8 Tu, 9 Tu, 10 Tu, 11 Tu, East 13 Tu, West 13 Tu, 15 Tu, Upper 16 Tu, Lower 16 Tu 正19图, 分19图, 殷6图(南玉圩), 推7图, 衣4图, 金2图, 22 Bao 43 Tu, 23 Bao 14 Tu, 24 Bao 16 Tu, 20 Tu, 21 Tu, 22 圆, 23 Tu, 24 Tu, 盖12 Tu, 14 Tu, 正15 图, 16 Tu, 2 区 17 图, 4 区 17 图. (Each map in the Yangjingtang Bridge Luxing Third District is exchanged at Zhang's House 45 Jingshang Temple Road, Laiyi Ferry, Pudong. All other maps except for Mansong Yangjingtang Bridge Luxing districts are exchanged at the Land Bureau in the city center) (End)

Sino-Foreign Famine Relief Committee Continues to Support Rural Relief Work 120

The Sino-Foreign Famine Relief Committee on Renji Road has always paid close attention to rural relief work. Last spring, the committee and the Ningbo Agricultural Relief Association jointly established the Ningbo Fangshan District Agricultural Improvement Cooperative, with a total of 132 cooperatives and 132 villages, serving 1,722 households. A total of more than 34,000 yuan was loaned out. Farmers received such economic assistance, their farms were enriched, and all were grateful. Considering the severe drought last year and the even worse spring famine this year, the committee decided to continue to lend the loans due last spring to agricultural improvement cooperatives near the capital to provide relief, which is a great boon for the rural areas.

According to Ling Daoyang, the chairman of the Ningbo Agricultural Relief Association, which cooperates with the committee, the use and distribution of the funds loaned out by the association last year are recorded as follows: 18,966 yuan for the purchase of cattle, 3,846 yuan for seeds and seedlings, 3,247 yuan for agricultural implements, 2,530 yuan for pig raising, 2,176 yuan for fertilizer, 1,506 yuan for fish farming, 1,275 yuan for agricultural product manufacturing, and 456 yuan for other expenses, totaling 34,002 yuan. He also said that because farmers will soon begin planting this spring, the most important thing is the lack of seeds. In addition to increasing the amount of loans for various items, the amount of loans for seeds and seedlings has been specially increased to ensure farmers' harvests. It has already been discussed and decided at a meeting a few days ago and will be implemented in a few days.

Chinese Tuberculosis Prevention Association Holds Second Solicitation Conference Yesterday; More Than Fifty People Attended, Including Mayor Wu; Mr. Lu Bohong Creates Tuberculosis Hospital 123

The Chinese Tuberculosis Prevention Association held its second solicitation conference at Mayor Wu's private residence on Haige Road at 3:00 PM yesterday. More than fifty solicitation team leaders, including Cai Jinjun and Li Tingan, attended. Mayor Wu hosted a tea party and issued membership application forms. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM after a group photo. The details are as follows:

Attendees: Yesterday's attendees included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Public Security Bureau Chief Cai Jinjun, Health Bureau Chief Li Tingan, Tuberculosis Prevention Association Solicitation General Captain Yan Fuqing, Deputy General Captain Lu Bohong, Bu Mei, Honorary Deputy Chairmen Wang Xiaolai and Xu Xinliu, Executive Directors Wu Liande, Xiao Zhiji's wife, Weng Zhilong, and Zhu Hengbi, Supervisors Du Yuexuan and Pang Jingzhou, Directors Ding Fubao, Liu Hongsheng, Pan Gongzhan, Wu Yunshu, Lin Kanghou, Li Dachao, Diao Xinde, Wang Xiaoying, and Ding Shujing, as well as solicitation team leaders Yu Zuoting, Lai Fengyan, Xi Guansheng, Zhang Xiangwen, Xue Cixin, Lu Ganchen, Liu Jisheng, etc., more than fifty people.

Chairman's Report: After performing the rituals, Chairman Wu Tiecheng reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that since the establishment of the association in December of the 22nd year, it has received enthusiastic support from everyone, and the association's affairs have gradually developed. However, the association deeply feels that this kind of movement cannot be successful overnight. 1.6 million people in China die of tuberculosis every year. It is only because there are 450 million people in the country that so many young and productive people are sacrificed, and it is not felt as pity as the death of an ant. We must know whether personal health will affect the health of the entire nation. National health requires a personal foundation. If we want to revitalize the nation, we must awaken the people and pay attention to tuberculosis. If you have tuberculosis, you become a scourge to the group. We must find a way to prevent it. Today is the beginning of the second solicitation conference. We hope to rely on the great efforts of all gentlemen and ladies, based on Shanghai, so that compatriots across the country pay attention to the great harm of tuberculosis, join the Chinese Tuberculosis Prevention Association, and fight tuberculosis together.

Li's Report: Then, Health Bureau Chief Li Tingan reported the work report and income and expenditure report for the past year, and reported the three-year plan. Immediately, he distributed membership application forms, 20 to each team leader, 10 copies of the association's charter, and 5 copies of the Healthy Movement Work Report and Plan (from the 23rd to the 24th year).

Yan's Speech: Then, Solicitation Team General Captain Yan Fuqing gave a speech, briefly stating that everyone is very clear about the significance of tuberculosis prevention. He recalled that there was a Mr. Xu who was a very prestigious person in society. He and his wife and five or six children were a very happy family. Unexpectedly, a few years ago, his wife died of tuberculosis in Changsha. Two years ago, Mr. Xu's eldest daughter (about 18 or 19 years old) suddenly contracted tuberculosis (hereditary) and died while studying in her second year of university, which made the family feel incomplete. Unexpectedly, six months ago, the second daughter also died of tuberculosis, also at the age of seventeen or eighteen, when she had just entered university. Mr. Xu was in great mental pain. What he knew was that two months ago, his son also contracted tuberculosis, but fortunately he was diagnosed and treated at the Jiangwan Sanatorium and did not have an accident, but is still in the hospital. From this point of view, the great harm of tuberculosis can be imagined, so we must actively prevent it, but prevention is difficult and requires money. Relying on everyone's strength, I will follow Mayor Wu and everyone else to actively prevent tuberculosis, the great enemy of mankind.

Lu Bu's Speech: Lu Bohong said in his speech, "In addition to the prevention opinions proposed by Mayor Wu, Dean Yan, and others, I also feel that there is a need for a 'large-scale tuberculosis hospital.'" Because chronic tuberculosis is a hundred times more difficult to treat than acute illnesses. It cannot be effective without years of treatment. In addition to founding a mental hospital, which will be completed in May of this year, I have planned to build a tuberculosis hospital near Beiqiao on the Shanghai-Minhang Road next spring, using more than 100 acres of land. Anyone with tuberculosis will be forced to be admitted to the hospital. If it is incurable, they will just stay inside to recuperate, so that they can be isolated from healthy people. The hospital is expected to accommodate more than 600 to 1,000 people. I hope that everyone will assist from the side." Finally, Dr. Bu Mei, the deputy general captain of the solicitation, gave a speech. His words were mostly warnings.

Request to Join: At the end, Mayor Wu hosted refreshments, and Mr. Wei Zhongle played a pipa solo. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM. The association also issued a request to join, stating, "Dear Sir, our association aims to promote the health of the people and prevent the occurrence of tuberculosis. Since its establishment, it has been more than a year, and we have received the support and assistance of gentlemen and ladies from all walks of life, so all plans can be gradually implemented. If we are given more manpower and financial resources, it will not be difficult for the pre-determined cause to 'be accomplished in three years'. Now, in order to promote the association's affairs, the team leaders have decided to lead the masses on April 6 to accomplish this great undertaking. All talents in the country will certainly agree. Therefore, we hope that you will generously donate a large sum of money to our association, or enthusiastically join us to help us, so that our association's cause can be promoted and enhanced, which will be truly beneficial to the future of national rejuvenation. Chinese Tuberculosis Prevention Association Second Solicitation Conference"

German Accuses Chinese National of Trademark Infringement in Film Business; Court Seized Many Cardboards; Hearing Concluded Yesterday Awaiting Sentencing 124

Zhang Shaojiu, a native of Wujin, Changzhou, founded the Dacheng Snap Button Factory in Jiangyin Village, Nanshi Jiangyin in the past year. It used the Four Five Brand trademark for a short period of time. Now Fucharkel, the German manager of the Wei Luibopo Premium Snap Button Company, has filed a lawsuit with the District Court Procuratorate against Zhang Shaojiu, accusing him of infringing on the company's Three Five Brand trademark by counterfeiting the registered trademark and infringing on exclusive rights. He requested severe punishment according to the law and requested permission to search and seize evidence. After receiving the complaint, the court instructed Prosecutor Xie Lian to send police to Jiangyin Village Dacheng Snap Button Factory to search and seize more than 9,000 Four Five Brand cardboards and summoned Zhang Shaojiu for interrogation and bail. A lawsuit was filed with the Criminal Court. At 10:00 AM yesterday, Director Zhang Peiming opened the twelfth court to hear the case. The plaintiff Fucharkel arrived in court with his private attorney Zou Yu.

First, Zhang Shaojiu said in his statement, "I am 28 years old. I registered with the Trademark Bureau in July of last year and founded the Dacheng Snap Button Factory. On September 3, I received the bureau's review letter, which considered it legal. Then, I submitted the Four Five Brand version to the bureau, which considered that the color and style were the same as the plaintiff's Three Five Brand and considered it inappropriate. Therefore, after receiving the review letter, I changed the color and style and did not imitate it. Please investigate."

Next, Fucharkel said in his statement, "I am 43 years old and a German national. Because counterfeit trademarks similar to the Three Five Brand were discovered on the market, sales fell sharply last year, reducing the transaction by 500,000 gold. The plaintiff's Three Five Brand snap buttons are manufactured in Germany and have been around for more than 30 years. Sales in China have also been around for more than 20 years. In July of the 20th year of the Republic, I applied for registration with the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. In March of the 21st year, I obtained the bureau's registration certificate, which stated that the exclusive right period was from March 15 of the 21st year to March 14 of the 41st year. Now, the defendant's Four Five Brand snap buttons, their decorations and the words on the bottom plate are the same as those used by the plaintiff, except for the extra 'Four Five' character. His intention to imitate and confuse the public is obvious. I request legal action."

Attorney Zou Yu rose to ask for a private prosecution, briefly stating, "The defendant's factory, such as various machines, probably requires 100,000 yuan of capital. Although it is a small commodity, the procedures are very complicated. Last year, the plaintiff's factory sold 500,000 gold less, which is a loss of more than 20,000 gold at 5%. The defendant should be ordered to compensate,"

At this point, Prosecutor Xie Lian rose to argue, briefly stating, "The defendant imitated the Three Five Brand trademark, the decorations and styles are the same, and more than 9,000 cardboards were seized in the defendant's home. The facts are clear, and I request a public judgment according to the law." The interrogator considered the case clear and the debate was concluded. The sentencing was scheduled for 10:00 AM on the 11th. The defendant Zhang Shaojiu was still released on bail pending further instructions.

Zhou Da: Sacrificed His Life for a Friend, Helping a Friend Chase After an Escaped Wife, Fatal Injury from Jumping off a Vehicle 125

Chang Fu-lin from Changzhou, 27 years old, married Li, a fellow villager, 18 years old, as his wife. They had children and lived by farming in their hometown. Unexpectedly, Li was not content with her marriage and secretly fled to Shanghai in April of last year. Under the pretense of being a domestic helper, she engaged in secret affairs and lived in hiding on the upper floor of a coal store in Tangjiawan, outside the West Gate. It was only recently that her husband found out her location, and he came to Shanghai in the middle of last month. He gathered several fellow villagers, including Zhou Ao-da (28 years old, residing at 23 Sanfu Lane, Xieshang Road, working as a tailor), and found Li. Because Li was unwilling to return home with her husband, they forcibly took her to the Second District Public Security Bureau to be sent to the General Bureau for investigation (previously mistaken for the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor's Office). After the Judicial Section reprimanded and advised Li, they ordered Chang to sign a guarantee and take her back to Changzhou. Fearing that Li would be stubborn on the way, on the 18th of last month, they hired car number 12567 from the Zhongxi Automobile Company at 465 Caishi Road in the French Concession, driven by the chauffeur Liu Dianqing, and went to the Public Security General Bureau. They again invited Zhou and others to accompany them, and took Li in the car, planning to go directly to the North Railway Station to take the train back to Changzhou. Unexpectedly, as the car drove past the Yongtai Xiang cigarette and paper store at number 144 on the corner of Route Lafayette and Route Pères Froc in the French Concession, the car slowed down to avoid vehicles and pedestrians crossing the road. Li seized the opportunity to jump out of the car to escape. At that moment, Zhou Ao-da, who was in the same car, also disregarded everything and suddenly jumped down to chase after her, causing both of them to lose their balance and fall, injuring themselves. This attracted onlookers who suspected it was a kidnapping or forced abduction of a woman. They immediately reported to the police station, and detectives were dispatched to send the injured to Guangci Hospital for treatment. Meanwhile, Chang and others were taken to the police station. After questioning by the police chief and investigation by detectives, Li's injuries were found to be lighter, and she was released and taken away by Chang. They then took the original car to the North Station to take the train back to their hometown. Details of this were reported in the newspapers on the first of this month. It is now learned that Zhou Ao-da suffered a severe head injury at the time of the fall and was hospitalized. Due to the severity of the injury, treatment was ineffective, and he died at 1:15 AM the day before yesterday. The hospital notified the police station, and detectives were dispatched to move the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Funeral Parlor for an autopsy. Zhou Jinrong (the deceased's uncle), the chauffeur Liu Dianqing, Dong Jiachuan, Dong Su-shi, and Li were summoned as witnesses. Yesterday, a report was submitted to the Second Special District Court, and the court-appointed prosecutor, along with coroner Jiang and clerk Peng, arrived at the scene. It was determined that the deceased, Zhou Ao-da, died from a head injury caused by jumping from the car. After questioning the witnesses about the circumstances of the incident, the court ordered the body to be released to the family for burial.

Chen Chang-gen: Chopped with an Axe While Sound Asleep, Fellow Villagers Committed the Heinous Act in the Middle of the Night, the Criminal Escaped and Only the Weapon was Recovered 126

Chen Chang-gen from Jiangxi, residing at 90 Burton Road, was sound asleep on the night of the second of this month when he was suddenly attacked by fellow villagers Zhong Peng, Fan Yunfei, and Xu Ji-kui, who broke down the door with an axe and dragged Chen out. Fan and Xu used flashlights to look at his face, preventing him from making a sound. Zhong pulled out a sharp axe and, without explanation, struck Chen's head, hands, and feet with several blows. Chen fell to the ground and cried for help. The perpetrators, seeing that their goal had been achieved, fled in a panic. Subsequently, Chinese detective Zhang Fa-xiang and Wang Run-he from the Hongkou Police Station arrived after receiving the report. Chen was found lying in a pool of blood, barely alive. He was taken to Tongren Hospital by police car for treatment. His injuries were severe, and he was unable to speak, making it impossible to identify the perpetrators. Around 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, it was learned that Fan Yunfei was hiding in a carpentry shop at 130 North Henan Road. Detectives Zhang and Wang, along with Western detectives, secretly went to the location and arrested him, taking him to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Lawyer Li Zhishan from the Municipal Council stated that the case originated with Chen Xu-sheng, a Jiangxi native who ran a woodworking shop on North Sichuan Road. He knew Zhong Peng and introduced a friend to work at his shop. Recently, the friend was dismissed, leading to a dispute over wages. Zhong invited several vagrants and took Chen Xu-sheng to a teahouse in Haining Village on Haining Road, where they harassed him and engaged in a verbal altercation. At that time, a Cantonese detective number 40 approached to inquire, but was slashed with an axe by Zhong's accomplices. The detective defended himself with his own pistol, and the group scattered like birds and beasts. It was later discovered that they were all members of the Jiangxi Club on Peng Road, known for their brawling. Police went to the club to make arrests, but they had already fled, and only several sharp axes were confiscated. Subsequently, the group suspected that Chen Chang-gen had informed the police, so they dispatched the defendants to secretly carry out the attack. The victim is currently seriously injured in the hospital and unable to appear in court. After the defendant was apprehended, he was taken to the hospital, where Chen Chang-gen identified him as one of the perpetrators. He requested a postponement for further investigation. When questioned, the defendant stammered and claimed that the perpetrators were Zhong Peng and others who were still at large. Judge Jiang Shu-zi ordered him to be remanded in custody for further investigation at a later date.

Investigation into Son-in-Law's Suicide by Drowning, Caused by Economic Pressure 131

At approximately 8:00 AM the day before yesterday, a man was found drowned in a well in the unfinished road of Shenjiazhai Road West, Datong Road, Zhongxing Road, Zhabei. After being discovered, it was learned that the deceased was Hong Wenzhong, 31 years old, a local man and the son-in-law of the Hong family at number 11. The deceased had an older brother, Hong Renjun, who lived at 41 Huide Lane, near Hanqiao, Qiujiang Road. The deceased originally worked as a telephone operator at the North China Company but was currently unemployed. He married into the Hong family on January 12th of the lunar calendar and was formally married on February 20th. His wife, Fengzhen, 18 years old, was working at the Puyi Yarn Factory but stopped working after the marriage. She only went to work the night shift on the 3rd of this month for two days. Unexpectedly, when she returned home from the night shift on the morning of the 5th, she learned that her husband had drowned himself in the well. She immediately reported it to police officer Zheng Zhiquan at post number 41, who reported it to the Xinzha Branch Bureau. Police chief Zhu Liming was dispatched to investigate and confirmed the incident. He instructed Shao Kuang, the local community leader, to report it to the Shanghai District Court for an autopsy. Yesterday afternoon around 4:00 PM, prosecutor Kong Xianglin arrived at the scene and confirmed that the deceased, Hong Wenzhong, had drowned himself. The family prepared a coffin for burial. According to neighbors, the deceased suffered from economic hardship after the North China Company closed down, causing mental disorder and leading to this unfortunate event. Yesterday afternoon, the Inspection Department of the Public Security Bureau also sent inspector Wu Yihong to investigate. It was learned that the Hong family had been widowed for three generations. Hong Fengzhen and the deceased had been married for only 23 days. Fengzhen's mother, Jiang, 42 years old, had been married to her father for only 13 days. Jiang's 72-year-old grandmother, Sun, is still alive, making them three generations of widows. There are no brothers or uncles in the same clan.

Dredging Bureau: Dredger to Arrive in Shanghai Soon, Already Left the Red Sea and in the Indian Ocean, Expected to Arrive Around the 15th of this Month 132

The world's largest dredger, ordered from Germany by the Shanghai Dredging Bureau, departed from Danzig on February 8th and is now two months into its journey. However, the ship is travelling slowly, and delays due to weather are unavoidable. Therefore, the expected arrival date in Shanghai is around the 15th of this month. A reporter from Datong News Agency has gathered the following information from the bureau:

Details of the Voyage from Germany: The ship was built by the German Xue Gao Shipbuilding Company. After completion, it departed from Danzig on February 8th, headed for China, and was crewed by Captain Johnsen and First Officer Arndt, dispatched by Xue Gao Company. The route is via the Kiel Canal, out of the Strait of Gibraltar, across the Mediterranean Sea, through the Suez Canal, across the Red Sea and the Indian Ocean, to Shanghai.

Expected Arrival Around the 15th: The Dredging Bureau received a radio message from the ship on the 3rd of last month from the Red Sea. It can now be assumed that the ship has left the Red Sea and is in the Indian Ocean. It should arrive in Shanghai around the 15th of this month. However, the ship was designed by Chief Engineer Cha, so Cha will first test its efficiency before formally accepting it and holding a naming ceremony.

Survey of the Shentan Completed: Rumors of two large dredgers being ordered from Germany are untrue. It is said that if another ship is needed for dredging in the future, it will only be considered after the currently ordered ship arrives in Shanghai and its performance is satisfactory. In addition, the Maritime Survey Bureau has completed the survey work of the Shentan (i.e. Tongsha Bar).
