Property Dispute of "Manure King," Old Accountant Also Accused, Existence of a Will is the Key Issue in the Case, Court Continued Hearing Yesterday to Obtain Statements from Various Parties 134

The late "Manure King" Ma Fuqi (also known as Gu Fuqi), who lived at 183 Weilanmeng Road in the French Concession, and his wife, A Gui-jie, made a fortune by contracting the sanitation business in the English, French, and Chinese areas. They accumulated a considerable amount of wealth, mostly in real estate. They had three sons: the eldest, Hong-kui, the second, Hong-sheng, and the third, Hong-gen. Hong-kui also passed away from illness last year, leaving behind a wife and concubine, as well as a son and two daughters. His wife, Ma Chen, has now filed a lawsuit with the Criminal Court of the Second Court, represented by a lawyer, accusing her third uncle, Ma Hong-gen, and his concubine, Ma Wang (also known as Wang A-da), of embezzling the estate and requesting an investigation. The court accepted the case, and Judge Qiu Huan-ying once held a hearing, summoning both parties for trial. The defendants also hired a lawyer to defend them. The presiding judge also personally visited

Important Witness in the Case: Wan Sanduo, the old accountant of the Ma family for many years, was questioned, and he turned over three keys. All of this has been reported in the newspapers. Yesterday morning, another hearing was held in this case. Both parties and their lawyers were present, and the audience was very crowded. Judge Qiu again presided over the hearing in Criminal Court 2. He summoned the parties to the front of the court and ordered the witnesses to leave the courtroom for separate questioning. First, he asked the plaintiff, Ma Chen, "What is the reason for accusing Wan Sanduo again?" She replied, "After my husband died, Wan Erduo opened the iron safe in the house without authorization and took five land certificates, loan documents, and mortgage documents from the safe, along with a coal ball factory passbook and two seals, and hid them." The judge asked, "Did your husband leave a will after his death?" She answered,

"There was no will. The will they presented to the court is forged." The judge asked, "Did your husband say how much property he had at the time of his death?" She answered, "He didn't say." The judge asked the defendant, Ma Wang, "How many keys did your husband give you at the time of his death?" She answered, "Two." The woman immediately handed them over to Wan Sanduo, and on August 25th, they went to the bank to open the safe and inspect the contents. The judge asked, "Did your husband leave a will?" She answered, "Yes, he did. My husband asked Lawyer Huang Zengjie to write it before he died. The will stated that my sister (i.e., the plaintiff Chen) and I would each receive 10,000 yuan, and the two daughters would each receive 5,000 yuan." The judge asked, "Where is the money specified in the will?" She answered, "I don't know." The judge asked the defendant, Ma Hong-gen, "Have you divided all of your inheritance?" He answered, "Not yet." The judge asked, "How much

property is there?" He answered, "I don't know. After my mother died, my eldest brother, Hong-kui, and Wan Sanduo managed it. After my eldest brother died, we wanted to settle the accounts." The judge asked, "Did Hong-kui have any personal property?" He answered, "I don't know." The defendant's lawyer immediately stated, "After Hong-kui's death, the two defendant brothers wanted to settle the property, but the plaintiff did not leave and even took her own son and daughters out. There is a fine letter from the Sino-French School as proof, so it was impossible to settle the accounts." At this point, the court summoned the witness Zhu Min-xuan, the assistant accountant, who stated, "I am 55 years old. I served as the assistant accountant in the Ma family starting on January 7th of last year." The judge asked, "Were all of the Ma family's documents under your custody?" He answered, "All of the documents were managed by the chief accountant, Wan Sanduo.

I only managed the payments. I don't know anything else." The witness Tan Keng-fu stated that he was a close friend of Ma Hong-kui. After Hong-kui died, he gave me three keys for safekeeping. Later, because of the land tax certificate from the Finance Bureau, I went with Chen, her younger brother Chen Guangyu, and Ma Hong-gen to open the silver safe. Chen Guangyu recorded everything." The judge asked, "What was inside the safe?" He answered, "It had nothing to do with me, so I didn't pay attention. Later, I gave the keys to Mr. Wan." At this point, the defendant's lawyer stood up again and said, "If Hong-kui was dying, why didn't he give the keys to his own people? Why did he give them to Tan Keng-fu? Please ask Mr. Tan about the reason for this." Tan answered, "This matter is

not convenient at the moment. I ask the court to understand everything." Then the witness Chen Guangyu (the younger brother of the plaintiff Ma Chen) stated, "Chen is my sister. I went with her when she went to the bank to open the safe. We opened three. The first one contained eleven or twelve bundles of banknotes, an ashtray, and some jewelry. There were also two boxes of gold weights. The second one contained Fangdan Dao deeds and other items. The third one was empty." The judge asked, "Did you record the jewelry and banknotes in detail?" He answered, "I made a brief record, but not in detail." The judge asked, "Do you know that Hong-kui handed over the sanitation business in the French Concession to Hong-gen with a written agreement?" He answered, "Yes, I do. I wrote the agreement." The judge gave this

copy of the document to Chen to read. The judge asked, "Is this how it was written?" Chen took it and looked at it and answered, "No, it is not. This is forged. Hong-kui only signed it, he didn't put a seal on it." As for the witness Yu Zhongming, he was not present at the scene. Ma Hongsheng was then summoned to the stand. According to his testimony, his eldest brother handed him his will before he died and told him to take care of his children. He is carrying the will with him now. After speaking, he took it out and presented it to the court. Lawyer Huang Zengjie stated that Ma Hong-kui, while dying, commissioned my law firm

to his bedside to record what he had set forth in his will. Later, my clerk transcribed it and I stamped it to certify it. Before Ma's mother died, she also commissioned me to write a will. Witnesses Zhang Quansheng, Yu Zhongming, Zhu Ruihua, and others were successively brought to court to testify. By this time, it was past noon. Judge Qiu stated that the facts of the case were complex and that a hearing would be scheduled for a later date after investigation. He told the lawyers representing both parties and the people involved that this case was a family dispute and that it would be best to resolve it out of court during the adjournment to avoid litigation. After speaking, he adjourned the court.

Rudeness and Homicide Case of Ni Yueqiu in Haimen Concluded; Sun Shenshi seeks Justice for her Husband 138

Ni Yueqiu, the former head of the Fifth District Office of Haimen, on the early morning of July 14th, 19th year of the Republic of China, led the district's security team members, along with Cheng Rusong, the captain of the county police team, to Changchun Town to arrest alleged communists. On the east side of the Dabai Temple in the town, a pedestrian named Sun Yuanfu was identified as a suspected communist and shot dead. The Haimen County Government sent personnel to verify that the deceased Sun Yuanfu had gunshot wounds to his left eye and chest, confirming that these wounds caused his death. On August 22nd, Captain Cheng Rusong of the county police team, based on a report from secret agent Liu Guanghan, learned that Chen Weirong, a resident of Qilin Town, was suspected of being a communist. He dispatched the leader of the third team, Jia Weiping, along with Ni Yueqiu, the head of the Fifth District Office, to Chen's residence, where Chen Weirong was arrested and taken to the county. Subsequently, Chen's son, Chen Zhouxiang, secretly invited Ni Yueqiu to Chong San Yi Inn and bribed him with a 1,000-yuan bank draft (from the De Kang Qian Zhuang) to plead with the county magistrate for his father's release. Soon after, Chen Weirong was indeed released. However, after some time, the county government, believing Chen Weirong was indeed a communist, extradited him to the Jiangsu High Court Prosecutor's Office. After investigation, the charges were dropped, and Ni Yueqiu was dismissed from his post. Fearing the consequences, Ni went into hiding in Shanghai. Sun Shenshi, the wife of the deceased Sun Yuanfu, learned of this and filed a complaint with the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor's Office. An order was issued to arrest and bring Ni Yueqiu to court. Prosecutor Ouyang Shu repeatedly investigated and confirmed the facts and prosecuted Ni Yueqiu on charges of dereliction of duty and murder. Yesterday afternoon, Criminal Court President Liu Enrong opened the court for trial. The plaintiff, Sun Shenshi, testified that she was 49 years old, from Haimen, and lived in Changchun Town. Her husband, Sun Yuanfu, had retired from the Ninth Army Quartermaster Department in the 19th year of the Republic of China and was soon after shot and killed innocently by Ni Yueqiu and others. She requested justice and compensation of 8,000 yuan in bereavement benefits, weeping as she spoke in a very tragic manner. The judge ordered the imprisoned Ni Yueqiu to be brought to the court, who stated that he was 39 years old, from Haimen, and denied the charge of shooting Sun Yuanfu. The defendant's lawyer then presented their defense. The judge considered the case closed and scheduled the verdict for 10:00 AM on the 12th of this month. Ni Yueqiu was remanded in custody pending the verdict.

Overview of Drought Relief Efforts in Gaochun 140

Gaochun News: The drought last summer was extremely severe in this county, affecting three-fifths of the county and impacting over 20,000 households. The area is traditionally poor, and the aftermath of the drought has left residents struggling. The county government formed an early disaster relief committee, uniting party and government officials and local gentry, and appealed to provincial authorities and charitable organizations in Shanghai and Suzhou. County Magistrate Yuan Jimei personally went to Shanghai and raised over 20,000 yuan in emergency relief funds, which were distributed to save those on the brink of starvation. They also secured 60,000 yuan for work relief, deciding to allocate 40,000 yuan for dredging rivers and 20,000 yuan for constructing ponds. The dredging of the Yaxi River, approved by the province, began on February 19th of this year. The river is 7.73 kilometers long and has been silted up for many years. Thanks to the efforts of all the workers, the project is progressing rapidly and is expected to be completed in mid-March. Currently, over 3,000 workers are employed daily. Each worker's relief funds, calculated to support a family of three, can help 10,000 disaster victims. After the river is dredged, the fields directly benefiting along both banks will amount to 13,350 mu. Assuming an annual value of 15 yuan per mu, the total value will be 200,250 yuan. The acreage indirectly benefiting from the irrigation of its tributaries is difficult to estimate. Furthermore, the previously submerged fields of Guanhudang will be completely dry, yielding over 2,500 mu of fertile land, increasing annual production by 25,000 yuan. Other benefits, such as land price and tax revenue, are too numerous to list. It is fitting that the local people are joyous and excited.

Apprentice Beaten to Death Case: Guo Liyu Sentenced to Eight Years; Guo Xiucai Acquitted 141

Wang Lianxiang, a 16-year-old apprentice from Nantong at the Xinwanxing pastry shop at 119 Xidou Road in the French Concession, went out at 7:00 PM on the 16th of last month to collect bowls and plates for pastries. While walking in front of 175 Malang Road, he accidentally bumped into Guo Xiucai (14 years old), the son of Guo Liyu (39 years old, residing above the mezzanine at 107 Ximenli, Ximen Road), a Anhui man selling cold glutinous rice. During their playful scuffle, Guo Xiu cai's head was injured, and he bled profusely. Guo Liyu, seeing his son injured and bleeding, rushed over and grabbed Wang, beating him with fists and feet, causing Wang to be injured and return to the shop, where he was bedridden. Guo then went with his son to the Xinwanxing pastry shop to demand compensation for medical expenses. After learning the reason, they sent Wang to Guangci Hospital and reported the incident to the French Concession police, who arrested the Guo father and son for investigation. Wang died from his injuries at 5:00 AM the next morning. The shop reported the death to the court, and the coroner's examination revealed that he died from internal injuries caused by the beating. The police handed the Guo father and son over to the Second Special District Court, where the police department filed a public prosecution against them for causing death by injury, according to the criminal law. This was previously reported. The case has now been concluded by President Wang Gangxu of the Second Special District Court after repeated hearings. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, President Wang ordered Guo Liyu and Guo Xiucai to be brought to the Criminal Court One, sentencing Guo Liyu to eight years in prison for causing death by injury, with eight years of deprivation of civil rights. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final will be used to offset the prison term at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. Guo Xiucai was acquitted. During the appeal period, both defendants will be held in custody.

Letter to the Editor 146

To the Editor, upon investigation of the "Resolution of Weights and Measures Disputes" item in the Wuxi Deshun column of your newspaper on April 6th, it stated that "rice merchants from six counties, including Wuxi, Suzhou, Kunshan, Yu, Wu, and Wu Jiang, lost a lot as Shanghai measures three he more than their own. The Wu Jiang County Government notified weight officials from eight counties to bring weights and measures to Shanghai for inspection, and to attend a meeting at the Inspection Office, chaired by Director Zhou of our office. After discussion, it was decided to re-determine the weights and measures tolerance and that this office would re-examine the weights and measures in this city by early May and submit them to the Ministry of Industry for record." Upon investigation, inspection officers from six counties including Wuxi visited our office on the second of this month for a private conversation only. On that day, Mr. Ni from Wu Jiang claimed that the five-dou measure in this city was three he more, requesting inspection. Director Gu was of the opinion that even if this was the case, the number three he was still within the legal inspection tolerance, so the director did not agree to the inspection request. The matter of re-determining the tolerance and submitting it to the Ministry for record is even more untrue. Correspondingly, we request that you correct the record. Please investigate and handle it accordingly. Sincerely, the Shanghai Weights and Measures Inspection Office, April 6th.

Special Advertisement

Business Report of the Kin Cheng Banking Corporation for the Year 1934 (22) 149

Among the various loans mentioned above, the Bank made special contributions in line with the purpose of assisting the national economy. These include food grain and cotton in agricultural products, cotton yarn in industrial products, coal in mineral products, and railway transportation in transportation services. Except for the railway transportation, which is described in another chapter, for the food grain, although imported rice accounts for only about 2.5% of domestic rice in recent years, its value is over 10 million yuan. Although imported wheat accounts for only about 4.5% of domestic wheat, its value is over 80 million yuan, resulting in a large outflow of capital. This is mostly due to the uneven distribution of domestic grain in different regions and the large price differences. Therefore, the Bank provides warehousing, collateral loan and remittance facilities for the collection and distribution of rice and grain, regardless of whether it is transported from farmers or grain merchants, wherever the Bank's institutions are located. In addition to serving rural areas, the Bank also hopes to make a slight contribution to the transportation and distribution of agricultural products. As for cotton yarn, it is related to the clothing of the people, and the outflow of capital to foreign countries has been very large over the years. In addition to providing considerable assistance to the competing weaving industry, the Bank also strives to facilitate the supply of raw materials, as the prices of cotton and yarn have been diverging in recent years, greatly affecting the yarn industry. For example, measures to promote the production, transportation, and sale of cotton are intended to assist agricultural production, as well as the textile industry. Coal is essential for industrial power and daily social needs. Coal is the most abundant mineral resource in our country, especially in North China. Therefore, the Bank has provided much assistance to major coal mines and has strived to promote the distribution of coal production to make it more socialized and popularized. By promoting sales and abundant production, the Bank directly and indirectly promotes the interests of this industry and its related aspects. B. Savings Department (A) Deposits (1) Total Deposits. The total balance of various savings deposits for the year 1934 was 43,281,406 yuan, while it was 31,678,629 yuan for the year 1933. This year's increase was 11,602,777 yuan. Analyzing and comparing: (A) The balance of fixed deposits was 33,708,405 yuan this year, and 23,638,261 yuan last year, with this year's increase being 10,070,144 yuan. (B) The total balance of current deposits was 9,572,001 yuan this year, and 8,040,368 yuan last year, with this year's increase being 1,532,633 yuan. (2) Number of Depositors. The total number of depositors for the year 1934 was 81,007. Analyzing: (A) Fixed deposits account for 46,435 accounts, accounting for over 57% of the total. (B) Current deposits account for 34,572 accounts, accounting for less than 43% of the total.

Educational News

Ministry of Education Orders Revision of Graduation Examination Regulations; Middle Schools and Normal Schools Abolish School Graduation Examinations; Semester Examinations Still Deeply Implemented in the Final Semester 150

(Nanjing, 6th dispatch) The Ministry of Education has issued an order to all departments and bureaus stating: "Having examined the current system where students in senior and junior high schools and normal schools must pass a school graduation examination before being allowed to participate in the graduation examinations. Only after passing the graduation examinations can they obtain graduation qualifications. Most graduates must also take entrance examinations for senior high schools and colleges or universities and can only continue their studies after being admitted. This requires junior high school students to undergo three examinations in a short period of time around the summer vacation of their final semester. The timing of the school graduation examination and the graduation examinations is very tight, and the subjects are the same. Furthermore, those who fail one or two subjects in junior high school are not issued certificates for applying to higher education institutions. Although they can apply to senior high schools with equivalent academic qualifications, the number of spots is limited. Also, there are no regulations on how to handle students who have been admitted to higher education institutions if they still fail the re-examination of one or two subjects. The Ministry has repeatedly considered all of these issues. In order to rationalize the examination system, it has been decided to abolish school graduation examinations in middle schools and normal schools (but junior high schools that do not participate in the graduation examinations or apply to higher education institutions should still hold school graduation examinations as before). Semester examinations will still be held in the final semester for the courses studied in that semester. The average grade for each academic year will be the school graduation grade. According to the regulations of the graduation examinations, it will be combined with the results of the graduation examinations. In addition, the issuance of certificates for applying to higher education institutions for those who fail one or two subjects in junior high school, and the method of remedial instruction for those who have been admitted to higher education institutions after failing one or two subjects, have been revised or supplemented in the original regulations. In addition to issuing separate orders to comply with the revised middle school and normal school regulations, and separate orders to comply with the middle school student graduation examination regulations and the normal school student graduation examination regulations (i.e., the revised provisional regulations for normal school student graduation examinations), you are ordered to comply with them and relay them for compliance."

Analysis of Subjects Studied by Students in National Vocational Schools 151

The Ministry of Education's statistics on the overview of national vocational schools and above in the 21st year have been reported previously. The following is an analysis of the subjects studied by students and graduates in higher education vocational schools and above (including universities, independent colleges, and vocational schools) in the 21st year.

(1) In the 21st year, the total number of students enrolled in vocational schools and above nationwide was 42,710 (universities: 25,635, independent colleges: 10,005, vocational school students: 343, vocational schools affiliated with universities: 1,084, affiliated with independent colleges: 2,555). By subject, the number of students in "science and engineering fields" was: science: 4,159 (universities: 3,855, independent colleges: 172, vocational schools: 31); agriculture and forestry: 1,557 (universities: 1,044, independent colleges: 189, vocational schools: 324); medicine and pharmacy: 1,852 (universities: 847, independent colleges: 637, vocational schools: 38); engineering: 4,439 (universities: 3,114, independent colleges: 899, vocational schools: 426). The number of students in "liberal arts fields" was: arts: 9,312 (universities: 5,909, independent colleges: 1,673, vocational schools: 1,712); law and politics: 4,523 (universities: 6,633, independent colleges: 5,153, vocational schools: 1,737); education: 3,368 (universities: 2,200, independent colleges: 663, vocational schools: 703); commerce: 1,867 (universities: 1,995, independent colleges: 485, vocational schools: 387).

The total number of graduates was 7,311 (undergraduate universities: 4,275, independent colleges: 1,240, vocational school students: 696, vocational schools affiliated with colleges: 842, affiliated with universities: 258). By subject, the number of graduates was: "University": science: 481, agriculture and forestry: 160, engineering: 602, medicine and pharmacy: 110, arts: 1,086, law and politics: 1,347, education: 241, commerce: 248. "Independent College": science: 16, agriculture and forestry: 21, engineering: 123, medicine and pharmacy: 117, arts: 93, law and politics: 647, education: 26, commerce: 87. "Vocational School" (including those affiliated with universities and colleges): science: 5, agriculture and forestry: 146, engineering: 150, medicine and pharmacy: 76, arts: 480, law and politics: 513, education: 209, commerce: 217.

(3) Comparing the past few years, the number of students in science and engineering fields has been increasing, while the number of students in liberal arts fields has been decreasing. The reason for this is the restriction on the number of students admitted to arts and law fields and the restriction on the establishment of law fields. Education must be adapted to actual needs, and educational authorities must strive to remedy the oversupply and lack of talent. Recently, not only has educational administration provided guidance and improvement for higher education in terms of the establishment of departments and the admission of students, but also the schools themselves have mostly changed to establish subjects that are adapted to the needs. Even students, in order to find jobs easily, pay more attention to selecting subjects.

(Zhenjiang Dispatch) The Jiangsu Province Normal School graduation examination is scheduled to begin on the 15th of this month. The examination hall rules have been formulated and are recorded as follows: Examination Hall Rules: (1) All examinees should bring their admission tickets according to the specified time and be seated in the hall according to the numbers assigned on the examination paper. Unauthorized changes are not allowed. (1) Examinees are not allowed to bring any paper scraps or notes, except for necessary stationery. (1) Examination papers of examinees who commit any of the following circumstances will be considered invalid: (1) Those who engage in cheating or are being cheated for; (2) Those who bring in books or manuscripts. (1) Points will be deducted from examinees who commit any of the following circumstances: (1) Talking and laughing with each other; (2) Engaging in any acts of passing or exchanging items; (3) Leaving their seats without permission. Examinees who commit any of the following circumstances should be immediately disqualified from the examination: (1) Disrupting the examination hall order; (2) Impersonating someone else. Disqualification will be limited to one subject, but if discovered more than twice, the examinee will not be allowed to participate in the examination in the current session. (1) Examinees should obey the instructions of the chief examiner and invigilators. (1) Examinees are not allowed to ask the chief examiner and invigilators about the meaning of questions or words. (1) Mathematics, physics, chemistry, and biology should be written in fountain pen. All other subjects should be written in brush, and all writing must be neat and clear. (1) Each examination paper will be provided with draft paper. Drafting on separate paper is not allowed. The draft paper and title page must be submitted with the examination paper. (1) Examination papers should be submitted according to the specified time and must not exceed the deadline. (1) The floating slip on the examination paper should be verified by the invigilator and removed on the spot. Examinees are not allowed to remove it themselves. (1) After submitting the examination paper, requests to add or modify words are not allowed. (1) After submitting the examination paper, examinees should immediately exit the examination hall and are not allowed to re-enter. The number of examinees in each district has been reported to the Education Department. It is estimated that there are 166 people in the first district of Zhenjiang, 226 people in the second district of Wuxian, 40 people in the third district of Rugao, and another 115 people in Nantong. There are 71 people in the fourth district of Tongshan.

Construction Method for the Annual Meeting of the Chinese Land Administration Society; The Central Government Actively Promotes Land Administration 153

(Nanjing, 6th) The second annual meeting of the Chinese Land Administration Society began on the 5th in Nanjing. The second general meeting continued on the 6th, passing a resolution to establish a Ministry of Land Administration under the Central Government and ordering all provinces, cities, and counties to actively promote land administration. Furthermore, regarding the current land policy in China, the society, after deciding through the second general meeting, summarized opinions from all parties and, after discussion and revision by all attending members, resolved as follows: The highest principle of our country's land policy is the equalization of land rights advocated by Mr. Sun Yat-sen. Although opinions on the interpretation of the equalization of land rights vary slightly, the understanding of the principle is generally the same. The theoretical basis of the equalization of land rights is that land should belong to all citizens. In other words, it recognizes that pure land rent should belong to the state and be implemented through land value tax and incremental value tax. The purpose is to seek an opportunity for all citizens to enjoy the rights and interests of land equally nationwide and to exclude private monopolies, using land as a tool for exploitation. Observing the current national economic situation and social organization, China's current land policy should pay attention to the following four points: 1. Quickly determine land prices and implement a progressive land value tax and incremental value tax to equalize the burden on the people, limit the power of the powerful, and prevent annexation. This will allow the state to collect land rent, the people to be freed from the oppression of harsh taxes, and the land to be fully managed, so as to promote the prosperity of the national economy and the peaceful development of society. 2. Immediately determine rental amounts based on the stipulated land prices, strictly enforce rental amounts, and, in the spirit of equality and cooperation, reform the tenant rent system to ensure a fair allocation of rights and interests between landowners and tenants, so that labor and capital can cooperate closely and each can benefit, rural areas can be stabilized, and the entire society can be expected to progress. 3. Implement the establishment of land financial institutions to regulate the rural economy, conduct land credit lending to encourage land development and support independent farmers, and supervise the use of land to integrate the intention of controlling land use, so that it meets the trend of national economic production and construction. 4. The state should immediately implement a land reclamation policy to regulate the distribution of land and population, develop wasteland, increase production, and enrich the border areas. The reclamation of border areas should be based on the principle of state-owned enterprises. The colleagues of this association believe that the above four points are the outline of China's current land policy and will strive to promote its realization.

The International Art Theater Will Hold a Lecture on Lawrence on the 12th; The Speaker is a Confidant of Lawrence 158

The first lecture will be held at 5:15 PM on the 12th of this month at the International Art Theater, No. 50 Nanjing Road. The speaker is Dr. Mohr, and the topic is "The Life and Works of D.H. Lawrence, a Modern British Novelist." The reason for Lawrence's success is that he wrote "Lady Chatterley's Lover," which nakedly depicts the state of love between men and women, similar to the style of novels such as "Jin Ping Mei" in China, but it is a new approach in European and American novels. Lawrence is an Englishman, and British society is still deeply secretive about the issue of sex. After the publication of Lawrence's works, it naturally caused an unprecedented reaction, and the book spread quickly, which was also expected. Dr. Mohr is not only Lawrence's doctor but also his close friend. In the two years before Lawrence's death, he was almost inseparable from him, so he has a thorough understanding of Lawrence's personality, his thoughts, his character, and his artistic tendencies. It is not an exaggeration to say that he is Lawrence's closest confidant. Because the International Art Theater has limited seating, those who want to attend the lecture should call 18843 to request admission tickets.

The German World Games Venue Will Be Completed This Year; The Grandstand Can Accommodate 20,000 Spectators... The Women's Dormitory Has Been Completed... German Athletes Receive Special Training... Help Find Excellent Positions 160

(National News Agency Berlin Dispatch) In 1936, the eyes of the world will once again focus on Berlin because the 11th World Games (Olympic Games) will be held in the German capital. This is not just a matter for Germany or Europe. So far, 41 countries have registered to participate. According to its significance, the venue should also have a huge construction to achieve the purpose of the conference. The reporter specially visited Dr. Timm, the secretary-general of the organizing committee, to inquire about everything. According to the conversation, as follows:

Huge Project

Dr. Timm said that the construction of the Olympic Games is proceeding actively according to the original plan. We must not underestimate it. The area of the venue is 130 hectares (one hectare equals more than one mu in China), and construction is required everywhere. Therefore, the construction of the venue is indeed a huge project. The foundation of the Dietrich Eck stand in the venue has been prepared in order and is expected to be completed this year, and then the interior construction will begin. The carefully constructed sports field can also be used. The foundation of the main venue and the path for the opening ceremony can be completed this winter, and the entire project can be completed by the end of 1935. The swimming pool has been started, and one part of the training ground has been completed. It has now been decided to open a red cinder track for the first time in Berlin. The Hochk Field (Hahoy) has started construction and a 76-foot-high clock tower is being built, with the Olympic bell hanging on it. This bell was donated by the Boehmer steel plant and has recently been cast. The racecourse has also been prepared for construction, and the stables will be built this year, and then flowers will continue to be planted and lawns will be laid. The most magnificent part of the construction in the venue is the Dietrich Eck grandstand, which can accommodate 20,000 spectators and has now taken shape and can be used for large-scale performances. There are also sports equipment facilities here, such as boxing competitions, etc. There is also a special competition venue paved with granite.

Women's Dormitory

Part of the women's accommodation in the sports field and one part of the sports meeting platform have been completed. In addition, a magnificent circular hall will be built in the German sports field. The design is made by the famous engineer Werner March and is gradually being implemented in reality, making Berlin the largest sports equipment venue in the world in 1936. German leader Hitler is very optimistic about various projects because he sees such progress in its construction in a short period of time. Although most experts have not completely resolved the various problems in it, we will find ways to solve such pending cases and coordinate the entire project. There are as many as 12,000 people currently working on this large project, and more people are needed this year. However, in addition to the purely construction-related issues, there is now the overall interior decoration, such as the program list should be printed in five languages. By 1935, when the conference office is built, the entire venue construction and everything else will be completed. Most of these issues have now been resolved. In short, our completion of the Olympic Games is not only the completion of external construction, but also all sports in the projects that should be carried out by the conference must do our best and strive to do it.

German Selection

The reporter also visited the director of the organizing committee, Busch, and asked about the selection and training of athletes. According to the conversation, our German Olympic competitors are still continuing training according to the original plan. However, this kind of training must pay attention to special performance when the Olympic competition officially starts. Usually, winter training is conducted at Hochk Field, and the finals are still held at this venue in summer. All Olympic participants will also train hard, and their highest form of performance can be obtained by 1936. Participants should continue to select the best under any circumstances, persevere and resolutely fight, because whoever has a determined heart must have a goal, and can achieve their goals in the Olympic venue, and those who can be selected as athletes have their own high reputation.

Special Training

Then give special teachings, such as circuit running or various light sports competitions, swimming competitions, and select the assumed champions of the country. It is most likely to happen. Each trainee trainer is responsible for the social standing obligations and must encourage the participants. For example, if some participants are still unemployed, they should be helped to find a suitable position, and better jobs should be given to those with excellent skills. This is indeed a psychological element of sports that we cannot ignore. However, this time, training must be carried out in order and legally. When performing in competitions, there are many actors prepared for each item, so they can be replaced and supplemented at any time, because in each actor team, they are not allowed to know whether they are participating in sports from beginning to end, so as to avoid unloading their psychological responsibilities. The competition procedures for 1936 will be implemented by the competition schools and review institutes. Because of the different sports, the review institutes are divided into various review groups, which are composed of experts respectively. If it is the Olympic preliminary round, the most outstanding representative team can be selected by the review group. The training results last year (1934) showed a significant increase because the route taken by each trainer was very correct. This is the evidence of its progress. However, the Olympic athletes in our country are still uncertain because the emerging athletes have a strong breakthrough. When the conference opens, there should be a leap forward. If each election has a solid position at all times, the old athletes will prevent the position of the newcomers and prevent their special efforts to maintain their own position. If the Olympic Games in 1936 opens, with our sure estimate, the various preparations will be more perfect.

Western Merchants Weak and Incompetent, Dong Hwa Wins Six to One, Strength Greatly Disparate, No Excitement, Dong Hwa Still One Point Short of Championship 163

After the unfortunate incident last week, the Dong Hwa football team was severely punished by the Western Football Association. Wan Xianghua, Chen Jiaqiu, and Lu Zhongen were all suspended. However, Dong Hwa has a wealth of talent and many reserves. Yesterday, they played against the Western Merchants in the Group A match at the Recreation Ground. The lineup was still vibrant and they defeated the Western Merchants by a score of six to one. With one more point, they will secure the championship. Yesterday, the weather was favorable, and more than five hundred people came to watch.

Lin Jingyi and Chen Yichen Successively Score

The match began, and Dong Hwa immediately took the offensive. After ten minutes, Li Yichen dribbled the ball forward, and the opposing inside defender committed a handball, resulting in a penalty kick. Li kicked it, but missed, and Dong Hwa lost a good opportunity. Then Li Yichen passed the ball to Dai, who lived up to expectations, received it and immediately shot, the ball entering from the left corner. Soon, Jia Youliang got an opportunity for a corner kick. Li Yichen couldn't wait and scored the second goal with a skillful volley.

Dong Hwa Takes the Lead in the First Half

After losing two goals in a row, the Western Merchants tried hard to counterattack. Forward O'er kicked fiercely at the goal, and the goalkeeper Guan caught the ball over the white line, resulting in a goal for Western Merchants. Later, the Western Merchants' lineup became disorganized again. Jia Youliang crossed from the wing, and A'Dai had no chance to shoot, so he passed it to Li Yichen, who indeed scored again. After that, Dong Hwa's offensive was quite strong. Li Yichen missed two good opportunities very close to the goal, which was a pity. At the end of the first half, Dong Hwa took a 3-1 lead.

Chen and Dai Score Again After the Break

After the break, they switched sides and continued the battle. Dong Hwa continued their efforts and attacked vigorously. The Western Merchants found it difficult to resist, allowing Dong Hwa to attack freely. Chen Chutian was still strong and vigorous, showing his past prowess, scoring two goals in succession. After a long scramble, Dai Linjing scored another goal, and Dong Hwa won 6-1.

Dong Hwa Missed Many Opportunities Yesterday

Overall, in yesterday's match, Dong Hwa lost three key players, but their strength did not diminish. Chen Yutian, as a veteran of the battlefield, was most praised by the audience. Gu Shangjiao also worked very hard yesterday, running around the field, showing extraordinary bravery. Li Yichen and Dai Linjing missed many opportunities yesterday, with potential for more than ten goals. Was this Dong Hwa's misfortune?

Dong Hwa Lineup

Guan Dang'an, Li Ning, Guan Xun'an, Gu Shangjiao, Feng Yunyou, Ding Qingxiang, Qian Zuozi, Li Yichen, Dai Linjing, Chen Chutian, Jia Youliang

Western Merchants Lineup

Municipal Education Bureau's Liao Dingju Plans District Primary School Sports Meet, Items and Grouping Standards Have Been Determined, Date and Location Will Be Announced After Approval by the Municipal Government 165

In order to promote physical education in primary schools in various districts of Shanghai and to facilitate the active participation of schools in various rural areas, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has decided to change the Municipal Joint Primary School Sports Meet to be held by district from this year onwards. It is said that it will be temporarily divided into eight districts. The Education Bureau is actively preparing, and will announce the rules, dates, locations, and other items after they have been submitted to the Municipal Government for approval. Primary schools in each district can make full preparations in advance according to the following items to avoid rushing at the last minute. (1) Track and field athletes, both male and female, are divided into three groups: A, B, and C. Group A is for those weighing 40.77 kg (90 lbs) or more, Group B is for those weighing 33.975 kg (75 lbs) or more but less than 40.77 kg (90 lbs), and Group C is for those weighing less than 33.975 kg (75 lbs). (Note) One pound equals 0.452 kg.

(2) Track and Field Events

Boys

Group A: 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, 800 meters, 80-meter hurdles, high jump, long jump, 2.718 kg (6 lbs) shot put, pole vault. Group B: 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, high jump, long jump, 1.812 kg (4 lbs) shot put. Group C: 50 meters, 100 meters, 200 meters, long jump, high jump, 1.359 kg (3 lbs) shot put.

Girls

Groups A, B, and C: 50 meters, 100 meters, standing long jump, 0.3048-meter (12-inch) softball throw. The sports items for each of the above groups may be appropriately changed by each district with the permission of the Municipal Education Bureau, depending on local conditions. (3) Each school with more than twelve classes may perform two sections of group exercises, and those with less than twelve classes may perform one section. (4) At least six-tenths of the students in each school must participate in the group exercises performance.

Investigation: Revival of Anhua Tea Industry in Hunan - Strong Russian Sales Drive Production - Last Year's Production and Sales Exceeded 80,000 Boxes 182

Historical Overview: Anhua is the most prolific tea-producing area among the 75 counties in Hunan province, holding a significant position in China's tea exports. Its tea production history dates back to the Xi Ning era of the Song Dynasty. Before Xi Ning, Anhua was part of the "Meishan Barbarian" territory, controlled by the Mei clan in the border region of Xinhua and Anhua. Xinhua was known as "Upper Mei," while Anhua was "Lower Mei." In the fourth year of Xi Ning, the Mei territory was conquered, and Anhua County was established, with tea farms set up. Tea produced in Yixi Mountain, Zijiang Benping, and other areas was considered superior in quality. A local saying at the time stated, "I'd rather eat Anhua grass than Xinhua's best," indicating that even the lowest grade of Anhua tea was superior to the highest grade of Xinhua tea. Tea trees grew naturally on the mountain and river cliffs. During the spring, many people were involved in tea picking and processing. The government stationed special officials to oversee the process, and the tea produced was offered as tribute to the capital, known as the "Four Bao Tribute Tea," with Daqiao, Xianxi, Longxi, and Jiuboshui designated as the "Four Bao." Each year, the county distributed funds (40-50 taels of silver) to local leaders at the Grain Gate to oversee production. The tea produced at the time was green tea and black tea. Green tea was sold in Hunan province and neighboring areas, while black tea, known as "Yin Tea," was sold in the northwest, including Shaanxi, Gansu, Xinjiang, and Mongolia. The name "Yin Tea" originated with Zuo Zongtang. In the early years of Guangxu, when Zuo Zongtang was campaigning in Xinjiang, he requested that the salt administration system be emulated, with 40 packages forming one "Yin," contracted to merchants for official sales. Most of the merchants entering the mountains to produce tea were from Wuyi, Fujian, as Fujian Wuyi tea was popular in the north at the time. When Fujian's production fell short, merchants rushed to Anhua to pick and process tea. Later, Shanxi merchants also arrived, forming their own group. The Shanxi-Jin merchants' guild hall still exists in Huangshaping today. The tea produced by these merchants was all black tea, sold in the Northwest. After the opening of the seas, Chinese tea was exported overseas, and foreign markets preferred red tea. As a result, during the Xianfeng era of the Qing Dynasty, Guangdong merchants came to Anhua to produce red tea, spreading the red tea processing method to local households. Subsequently, due to the strong sales and good prices of red tea, most tea merchants switched to producing red tea, including those from Shanxi who had previously specialized in black tea. The production and sales of red tea were most developed during the Guangxu era. At that time, there were over 80 tea houses in Dongping, Gaokou, Huangshaping, and Xizhou, producing 700,000-800,000 boxes of tea annually. Later, due to failures in the export trade, production gradually decreased to 400,000-500,000 boxes, then 300,000-400,000 boxes, and before the European War, only 200,000-300,000 boxes. After the European War, during the 7th and 8th years of the Republic, the industry was severely depressed, with tea mountains barren and desolate. Tea merchants then switched back to producing black tea for sale in the Northwest. In the 12th and 13th years of the Republic, the red tea market showed signs of recovery, and in the 15th and 16th years, some tea mountains were reclaimed. However, after China and Russia announced the severance of diplomatic relations in the 16th year of the Republic, Russian merchants could no longer directly purchase tea in Hankou, and the sales of red tea to Russia stagnated. Although British trading houses in Hankou continued to handle some shipments to Russia, the volume was much lower than direct trade. As a result, the industry declined again. Last year, when China and Russia resumed diplomatic relations, Russian merchants came directly to Hankou to purchase and transport tea, and all the accumulated stock of tea merchants was sold out. The price of #3 tea exceeded that of neck tea, and the volume of sales reached 40,000-50,000 boxes. Some tea houses made profits of 20,000 yuan or several thousand yuan. Last year, the number of tea merchants entering the mountains to produce tea increased slightly. There were over 30 red tea merchants in Dongping, Gaokou, Huangshaping, Youzhou, Jiangnan, and Xiaoyan, producing over 10,000 boxes of red tea. It is expected that the number of tea producers will increase even more this year.

Tea Planting Overview: Anhua is divided into two districts, the front and back. The most abundant tea-producing areas are all in the back district, centered on Dongping and Huangshaping, followed by Youzhou, Jiangnan, Xiaoyan, Bianjiang, Lantian, and Xianxi. The terrain is characterized by layered mountains and very little flat land. The soil is yellow and ocher sandy loam and clay loam. The total tea planting area is approximately 100,000 mu. The tea trees are generally of native varieties, with small trees, thick and soft leaves, and mostly triangular seeds. For propagation, seeds are collected before the Cold Dew solar term and sown in nurseries either at that time or in the following spring. After two years, they are transplanted to the main garden, but some also directly sow seeds in the main garden. In terms of management, the land is generally plowed once in the autumn when weeds have not yet withered. Very few people use fertilizer. Intercrops include peas, broad beans, soybeans, corn, buckwheat, sugarcane, and peanuts. Leaves are harvested twice a year, after Grain Rain and after Mangzhong. The yield per mu is approximately one hundred jin.

Tea Processing Overview: (1) Red Tea: In the preliminary processing of red tea, fresh leaves are sun-dried until properly withered, then swept together and kneaded until the leaf juices are fully extracted. The clumps are then broken up, air-dried, kneaded again, and dried again. They are placed in barrels, covered with cotton, and fermented for a period of time until the color turns reddish-brown, at which point they can be sold. However, some are dried further. This is the initial processing method. The refining process is more complicated. After tea merchants receive the raw tea, they first roast it once for about 15 minutes, adjusting the time based on the dryness of the raw tea. After roasting, the tea is stored in official warehouses for about two to three days, then fired again, called "re-firing." After re-firing, the tea is loaded into loose boxes, taken upstairs, and manufacturing begins. Initially, a coarse "rain" sieve is used to sift out the raw tea beads. After being rubbed with a sieve, it is re-sieved. The tea from the bottom of this sieve passes through a raw tea "long horse" sieve, using a nine-level sieve to "scoop". The tea from the surface of this sieve is called "raw tea neck." After firing and drying, it is crushed and sieved again. The tea from the bottom of this sieve is divided into first tea, second tea, third tea, fourth tea, coarse rain, medium rain, bud rain, iron sieve and raw powder, where raw powder is flower fragrance, the material from the bottom of the ninth sieve, with a shape like powder. All these types of tea except raw powder, are then placed in a wind machine. The powder sorted out by the wind machine, is immediately discarded or mixed in the flower fragrance. The remaining tea, is loaded into loose boxes and brought downstairs, where female workers are responsible for picking selecting, called "raw picking." After this raw picking, it is brought upstairs and sifted again with the sieve surface being clear tea pearls which are natural pearl tea. The bottom of the sieve is sorted into original body, neck, second, third, and fourth tea, and coarse rain, medium rain. After "sifting" and scooping again, the sieve face is clear tea head. The sifted original body tea, is taken downstairs for repeated selection, then a wind machine is used to blow away the ash, then one more firing is done before sorting and packing into boxes to complete the manufacturing. Last year's red tea production was 42,600 boxes of boxed tea, 1,500 packages of raw red tea, 2,600 packages of flower fragrance, and 1,000 packages of tea stalks.

(2) Black Tea: Anhua black tea is mostly produced in Jiangnan, and the best quality comes from Huangshaping. In the processing method, fresh leaves are put into a wok and stirred with a three-pronged fork until the leaves wither, soften, and become like cotton wadding. They are then taken out of the wok and piled on the floor, where they are trampled until the leaf juices are fully extracted. The clumps are broken up after approximately three times and then taken out and roasted in a drying rack to dry. Black tea is a coarse tea, ranging in length from an inch to a foot. Production is divided into yellow and black types. The black type is sold in Shaanxi, known as "Shaanxi Yin," and the yellow type is sold in Gansu, known as "Gansu Yin." These are all referred to as "Yin packages." The best quality teas are wrapped in palm bark, called "Flower Rolls," and bundled into branches using bamboo strips, each branch weighing 1,000 taels. These are mostly sold in Shanxi. Black tea is generally sold in the northwest provinces and Mongolia. Nowadays, some is also sold to Soviet Russia. Last year's production was 13,000 flower rolls and 15,000 large packages (each package weighing 140 jin). In the past ten years or so, due to poor sales and low prices of red tea, most farmers have switched to producing black tea, as the processing method is simple and the tea can be stored for a long time, waiting for a better price. The production of red tea has gradually decreased.

(3) Green Tea: Anhua green tea is produced in Qiaotouhe and Lantian. The crude processing method does not require fermentation, and the refined method is largely similar to that of red tea: (1) stir-frying leaves for about four minutes, (2) kneading for fifteen minutes, (3) breaking up the clumps and air-drying for five minutes, (4) re-kneading for ten minutes, (5) breaking up and air-drying for three minutes, (6) re-kneading for fifteen minutes, (7) drying for twenty-five minutes. Last year's production was about forty shi, priced at around 30 yuan per shi. The tea is generally shipped via Meijiang to Xiangxiang, Ningxiang, Changsha, and other places for sale, with no sales to other provinces.

Tea Merchant Overview: Anhua tea merchants are generally composed of capitalists from Shanxi, Guangdong, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hunan provinces, divided into the Xi (Shanxi) group, Yue (Guangdong) group, and Xiang (Hunan) group. Those from Hunan are called the "local group," while those from other provinces are called the "guest groups." The Xi group (Shanxi) has the most disciplined organization and the strongest capital. Most of their organizations adopt a shareholder system, with very few being operated by a single person. The capital of each firm ranges from several thousand to over ten thousand yuan, specializing in buying raw red and black tea, refining it, and transporting it to Hankou for sale. Black tea is then transported to the northwest via the Pinghan Railway. There are a total of 28 trading houses, which provide tea warehouses, manufacturing equipment, and assistance to merchants in buying tea, charging 57 wen per thousand. In terms of taxes, garden owners pay 13% for group defense, community security, township administration, industry, and charitable donations. Tea merchants pay 1% as a business tax, with a silk tax revenue of around 60,000 yuan last year. Tea merchants traditionally use a 76% scale for raw tea (i.e., every 100 jin is counted as 76 jin), even though the actual discount need not be so high, but due to old habits, it is difficult to change.

Supply and Demand of Jiaoji Railway Coal 183

The recent supply and demand trend of Shandong coal, especially Jiaoji Railway coal: Several years ago, due to political instability and the decline of various industries along the railway line, supply and demand were both around 2 million tons. However, later, as the political situation gradually stabilized and various industries along the railway line recovered, the demand for coal increased. In addition, after the protection tariff was raised in May of the previous year, Japanese coal and Fushun coal gradually decreased, replaced by domestic coal, i.e., a sharp increase in the demand for Jiaoji Railway coal. Especially the excellent quality Boshan coal, this should have been a period of active demand. However, the domestic coal mines have immature equipment and cannot fully meet this demand, which is a great pity. Recently, although each mine has plans to expand equipment to increase production, whether this can be realized in this era of difficult financing is a question.

On the other hand, although Zhongxing Coal's production could not be satisfactory due to political instability (more perfect equipment) and various other factors several years ago, since the political situation has changed, it has proceeded according to its set plan. Currently, annual production is increasing and has now exceeded one million tons per year. As mentioned above, there are still no great expectations for the output of Jiaoji Railway coal in the future. However, the demand from the railway line and the coastal ports continues to increase, and there is currently a shortage. If there are no major changes in tariffs in the future, the demand for Jiaoji Railway coal and Zhongxing Coal in the Shanghai market will inevitably increase sharply. Based on the supply capacity of these three (Jiaoji Railway Coal, Zhongxing Coal, and Kailan Coal), the competition in the Shanghai market in the future will not be too fierce. From a general economic perspective, all industries in the world tend to decline, and the coal mining industry will inevitably decline along with them. However, at present, due to special reasons such as insufficient supply, tariff protection, and urgent needs at coastal ports, it may not fall into decline at the same time. The following table lists the production, transportation, and other conditions of Jiaoji Railway coal in the past five years.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

The Meaning of Our National Flag 184

— Qián Chuò Héng Jiǔ

Dear Children! If someone asks you, "What does our national flag look like?" I believe you will quickly answer, "Blue Sky, White Sun, and a Red Ground." But if they ask you again, "What is the meaning of our national flag? Who created it?" I think many of you may not be very clear about it, right? Now let me tell you:

Our national flag was created by the revolutionary martyr Mr. Lu Haodong before the Guangzhou Uprising. The blue, white, and red colors on the national flag represent freedom, equality, and fraternity. The twelve corners of the white sun represent the twelve two-hour periods of the day: Zi, Chou, Yin, Mao, Chen, Si, Wu, Wei, Shen, You, Xu, Hai.

Children! Do you all understand the meaning of our national flag now?

Faraday's Childhood 185

— Jūn Péng

Children! Who invented the generator? Everyone knows it was the great American scientist Edison, that's right, but how could Edison and others have used it to create electric lights, streetcars, telephones, and all kinds of electrical machinery? Well, that's because of this Faraday! Because many people in the world know about Edison, but few know about Faraday, so I'll tell you a little about his life for you to listen to!

Faraday was the son of a blacksmith, so of course the family was not well-off, and he didn't study; it had nothing to do with blacksmithing; how could Faraday be sent to school to study! At the age of thirteen, he began to work as an apprentice with Libo to learn bookbinding, and did so for seven years. This apprentice had a very strange temperament, reading books while binding them; during this period, he bound an encyclopedia, and there was an essay in the book entitled "Electricity," and he cherished a grand ambition to attack electricity, so he saved money and bought instruments and chemicals to do that kind of chemical trick.

One day, he heard that the Royal Society's famous chemist, Mr. Dai Pei, was going to give a public lecture in London. At that time, a customer came to buy something from him, and he asked this customer if he would be willing to do the favor of inviting him to London to listen to the lecture. The customer readily agreed and bought four admission tickets for him. Faraday went to the city to listen to the lecture, writing down notes as he listened, and when he returned to the shop, he wrote a long letter to Dai Pei, and showed him the notes, requesting an interview. Later, Dai Pei wrote back inviting him to talk, and at that time he also asked to work at the Royal Society, so that he could study science. Finally, he invented the generator and its principle. Faraday was undoubtedly the founder of the electrical world.

Good Baby 186

— Xià Zhōng Hàn

Little baby, body good,

Get up every day and learn gymnastics,

Daddy sees it and laughs,

Mommy sees and calls "Baby!"

Laughs, calls "Baby!",

Stick out the little chest and run forward,

Strong body, lofty ambition, avenge national hatred,

Blue Sky White Sun flag flutters!

Science Mr. Bends Magic 187

— He Gongchao

Red and Black Separate Families

One warm spring, Science Mr. appeared on stage again. He held a horseshoe-shaped thing in his hand, raised it and said to the audience:

"Children, do you know what this is? This is a horseshoe magnet, commonly known as a 'magnet'. Its property is that it can attract steel. Today we are going to use it to do a very interesting magic trick."

After he said that, he took out a plate, a file, and a rusty nail from his pocket. Then he filed the rusty nail with the file for a while, and the plate was covered with black iron filings and red rust powder. He shook the plate a few times to mix the two things.

"Now, this red iron powder and black iron filings are one family." Science Mr. said, "But we have to separate them, red with red, black with black. Children, do you have any appropriate methods?"

The children in the audience all shook their heads, feeling that such tiny things could not be picked up by hand, nor could they be used—there was simply no way.

"Haha! Nothing could be easier! You see..." Science Mr. picked up the horseshoe magnet and brought it close to the bottom of the plate. Sure enough, the black iron filings jumped up one after another and adhered to the head of the horseshoe magnet. The head of the horseshoe magnet suddenly looked as if it were covered with fine hairs, which was very beautiful.

"Now, the black ones are all attracted to the horseshoe magnet, and the red ones are all left in the plate. This is called 'Red and Black Separate Families'."

Then there was a round of applause from the audience.

"Why can horseshoe magnets only attract iron filings and not rust powder? It turns out that in humid air, the oxygen in the air combines with the iron on the nail to form rust. At this time, the properties of rust are different from the properties of iron; therefore, the horseshoe magnet cannot attract it."

"If you want to perform this magic trick, a horseshoe magnet is indispensable. You can buy it from instrument stores—the Science Instrument Museum on Fourth Malu in Shanghai—for eighty or ninety cents each. With this horseshoe magnet, we can also play many other kinds of magic tricks; I will show you these next time."

— A Hua wrote

Facing Mr. Chen's face

Min'er's Luxury Fake Travel Plan 188

— Linghu Zhao

How fast time flies, in the blink of an eye, the annual travel season—spring break is here again!

Children, you have at least ten days to play during this spring break. You must not waste this great time in a rush. So, will you bury your heads in books all day during the spring break? No, absolutely not. These days of rippling spring air and beautiful spring scenery are not suitable for studying all the time. We should visit Qingxiu, majestic famous mountains, or historical sites to travel. This can not only comfort our body and mind, but also increase our knowledge. The wonderfulness of Sima Qian's articles is entirely obtained from travels.

Now let me introduce Min'er's travel plan for your reference.

(1) Monday, go to Longhua with mom, and take the opportunity to visit the Longhua Airport once.

(2) Tuesday, invite Zhang Jian to go to the field to fly a kite.

(3) Saturday, my brother has nothing to do when he gets home in the afternoon, I ask him to take me to the park.

(4) Sunday, Dad accompanies me to Jiangwan, Wusong and other places to travel.

(5) Others, decided temporarily. Children, you can also design and implement it yourself.

Dust 189

— Bing Yu

We clean the house every day. Fine dust is invisible to the human eye in dark places. If it is in a place exposed to sunlight, you can see dust scattered in the air. This many dust looks like it is flying very lightly in the air, but in fact it is mixed with water droplets, sand flakes, metal shavings, microbes, sanitary insects and other things, so it is not light. Water is seven hundred times heavier than air, and there is a lot of water floating in the air, but if the water droplets are as big as raindrops, they will fall very quickly. If the diameter of the water droplet is one tenth of a millimeter, its falling speed will be three seconds; if the diameter is one hundredth of a millimeter, the falling speed will be five minutes; a water droplet with a diameter of one thousandth of a millimeter will take eight hours and fifteen minutes; and a water droplet with a diameter of one ten-thousandth of a millimeter will take eight hundred hours. Fog is transformed from water, and the falling speed of fog is between five and ten minutes. Dust originally exists in various parts of the room and scatters into the air due to the vibration of the wind, but because there are various substances in the dust, the falling speed is also very different. The heavy ones will fall to the ground in one or two seconds, and the light ones will still be scattered in the air after a day or a month and cannot fall. Therefore, when we clean the house, we should open more windows and ventilate the air, so that the dust stirred up by brooms, chicken feather dusters, and bricks in the room can be blown out of the windows by the outside wind. However, we clean the room every day, and although the heavy dust gradually falls to the ground or because it is on the walls and other utensils, the light dust flies in the air for a day or two because the falling speed is very slow. Then, it can be said that there is dust flying in the room all year round.

— (Yi She)

I am studying how to make paper umbrellas after the "Labor" class.

Why Do You Feel Cold After Exercise? 190

— Hua Nan

Children! Let me ask you: After you exercise, sweat, and after a while, why do you feel cold?

Children! Please think about it first, and then read my answer.

It turns out that after you stop exercising, sweating stops. But what about the sweat that has already come out? It evaporates, and when it evaporates, it needs a lot of heat, and this heat is absorbed from your body, so you feel cold.

So, children! When you exercise, you must not take off your clothes again because of the heat. You should wait a few minutes and then put on the clothes you took off, otherwise you will catch a cold.

Making Solid Regular Polygons 191

— Cheng

Tools—knife, copper edge ruler, cardboard, paste, various colored craft paper, and scissors. Method—(1) Cut out each figure (attached later) in order and paste it on cardboard.

(2) Draw each figure (pasted on cardboard) separately.

(3) Use a knife to cut a deep mark along the dotted line on the figure until it is half the thickness of the cardboard.

(4) Use the same method to cut a deep mark on the narrow side and the figure itself.

(5) After the above procedures are completed, gently fold the marked areas and use paste to glue the narrow side to the nearest surface. In this way, the pattern of the polygon is set, and then paste various colored craft papers to make a very good toy produced by our factory; take it to your children, and you will definitely receive a warm welcome.

The Course of Bitter Son 192

— Zhang Mengzhao

Children's Day has passed! What should we feel?

The children of wealthy families and the bitter children wandering the streets clearly divide the joys and sorrows from wealth and poverty! Children's Day seems to be decorated for aristocratic families! Poor children from poor families. Don't feel anything? I am also a member of the bitter children's team. I remember when I was young, I received education and baptism from my loving mother's hands. Although the school was three to five miles away from home, I still had to walk! In rainy and snowy weather, in order to avoid wading, I only brought some coarse rice flour? Hiding in a corner of the school kitchen, I asked the chef for a little boiling water to mix and use as lunch. Sometimes I bought some sweet potatoes to satisfy my hunger, regardless of people's ridicule! The students who went to school had money for meals in the school. At that time, although I was very sad! But I was determined to study hard! In every school exam, I was always at the top of the list. So I firmly believe that people's hands and brains are omnipotent! "Accumulating wealth of thousands is not as good as having a skill." I advise the bitter children comrades now, you must know the true meaning of Children's Day! Strengthen your bodies, work hard in your studies, and strive to emerge from difficulties and hardships! Achieve economic independence and have the ability to create careers for the happiness of the masses!

The Adventures of Sinbad the Sailor (12) 193

— Xin Qing

Sinbad's Fourth Voyage

The joy of my family life soon eliminated the fear in my heart. Before long, I set off again, this time taking the route through Persia, doing business on one hand and seeing the unseen scenery on the other.

Finally, I arrived at a port, and from there I set sail with my goods. We entered ports everywhere, and my goods sold very well, and in a short time I had unloaded almost everything I carried.

One day, far from the land, a strong wind suddenly rose. Although everything was done to protect us, the ship soon became a wreck, and several lives were lost.

My good luck was again in my favor, because I grabbed a board, on which several friends were already riding. We were swept by the tide to the shore of a small island, just in a high and dry place.

There we found fruit to eat and a clear spring to drink from. We stayed on the shore all night. But when the sun rose the next day, we got up and set off, walking towards several huts that looked very far away from us.

As we approached, a group of black people came up and took us to their homes. They made us sit down and gave us an herb; they gestured to us, saying that we could eat this herb.

My friends ate as they were told, but I saw that the black people did not eat, so I thought it must be a trick to harm us. I did not eat mine, and it was good that I did not eat, because my poor friends soon lost consciousness and did not know where they were or what they were saying.

Then the black people fed us rice and oil to eat. My friends ate a lot, but I did not eat much, because I had already seen through these plans. The herb was to deprive us of our will and power of movement, and the rice was to make us fat—because these black people were cannibals.

Soon I felt that my thoughts were right, because they ate my friends one by one, but I was too thin and did not touch me. They gave me freedom to wander near the hut, but the thought of fear of death made me thin day by day, but they wanted to wait for me to get fat before eating. My unhealthy body became my greatest benefit, and my life was saved because of it.

One day I strayed a little far from the hut and decided to escape. At that time, there was only an old man near the house, and I did not care no matter how much he called.

Children's Science Lecture: Types of Vegetables 194

— Lin Yin

Children, don't you always have vegetables with your meals every day? There are many types of vegetables, but when we eat them, we always eat their roots, stems, leaves, and fruits. Some vegetables can be eaten for their vegetables, roots, or fruits. Some vegetables can only be eaten for their roots but not their leaves. Ordinary vegetables have the following four distinctions.

(1) Leafy vegetables: We mainly eat the leaves of this type of vegetable. Although the other parts can sometimes be eaten, they are not the main parts. Like the cabbage and rape in (Figure 1), we see that the leaves are very fat, but the stems can also be eaten. Onions and garlic cannot distinguish between stems and leaves, but they are generally included in the leafy vegetables.

(2) Root vegetables: The leaves and stems of this type of vegetable cannot be eaten, because their nutrients are all in the roots, and the roots are very developed and fat. As shown in (Figure 2), onions, sweet potatoes, radishes, and turnips belong to this category.

(3) Stem vegetables

This type provides us with a part of the stem for food. The lettuce, celery, and wild rice shoots shown in (Figure 3) are all examples. Although their leaves also grow very lushly, their taste is not as good as the stems.

(4) Fruit vegetables

The roots, leaves, and stems of this type of vegetable cannot be eaten, but their melons and fruits taste very good. The pumpkins, boxes, spicy eggplants, and cattails shown in (Figure 4) are all eaten for their fruits.

Children, when you eat vegetables, can you tell which part of the vegetable is provided for us to eat? This is a very interesting research question!
